Liao Chengzhi Arrested in the Concession 124

Reportedly the Son of Martyr Zhongkai

His Mother He Xiangning Telegraphed for Rescue

Soong Ching-ling Visited and Comforted Ms. He Yesterday

Liao Chengzhi, the son of Central Committee member He Xiangning, was arrested by the Old Gate Police Station the night before last, suspected of being a communist. The reporter of the Nisshi News Agency specifically visited Ms. He at her private residence to inquire about the matter, and she answered in great detail. The details are recorded below.

Dropped Out of School and Returned to China 125

Ms. He said that my son Chengzhi is 26 years old this year. He went to Germany in the 18th year of the Republic to study political economy. He has not yet graduated. Recently, because he was indignant about the violent Japanese invasion and the increasingly urgent national crisis, he believed that it was time to dedicate himself to the country, not to sit idly by and study. So he angrily returned to China. It has only been two weeks since he arrived in Shanghai. I have been ill recently. My son, having returned from overseas, often attends to me. He usually tells me about his father, Mr. Zhongkai's loyalty to the country and the tragedy of his martyrdom, urging him to work hard for the Party and the country and not to disgrace his father's legacy. My son has also been able to deeply understand this meaning and study hard. I did not expect that only two weeks after returning to China, this unexpected event would occur. What else can I say?

Arrest Process 126

It is reported that the Old Gate Police Station received a report in advance that my son was a communist. Five foreign armed detectives and two Chinese armed detectives went to No. 8 Wufu Lane, Shanxi Road, and took my son and two others (namely Luo Dunxian and Yu Wenhua) into a car and drove them to the police station for detention. At that time, there was no evidence. After the arrest, with the permission of the police station, at about 11:00 the night before last, five Western policemen and two Chinese policemen were sent by the police station in a car to accompany them home to see me and explain their wrongful arrest. The Western policemen also asked me if I was their mother before returning to the police station. I was extremely shocked and pained by this incident. I then thought that the country has its own laws. Whether my son is a communist or not, there are facts that can prove it and the law can resolve it. At this time, I will remain silent and not say a word, but ask for an early resolution in accordance with the law so that he will not be detained in a foreign prison for too long.

Engage a Lawyer 127

Ms. He concluded by saying that this case can be resolved by our country's own laws. After it is transferred to the court, she intends to engage Lawyer Wu Kaisheng to defend him. The truth of this case will be revealed soon.

Telegraph to the Whole Country 128

To the military and political leaders of the whole country: My son Chengzhi was arrested by a foreign police station in Shanghai last night, but I do not know where he is being detained. I am willing to stay in prison with my son, but I do not want to stay in a foreign prison. I request to be transferred to the Chinese area. I am willing to die in the Chinese area, not in the concession. Please investigate and reply. He Xiangning. She also telegraphed Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Jingwei, T.V. Soong, Sun Ke, He Yingqin, and others, with similar content. In addition to sending telegrams, Ms. He has also asked the municipal government to quickly negotiate with the Old Gate Police Station and transfer him to the Chinese court for trial in accordance with the law as soon as possible to show prudence.

Wang Replies to Ms. He's Telegram 129

Wang Jingwei replied to Ms. He Xiangning's telegram, "Dear Mrs. He Xiangning, I have respectfully received your telegram. I have not known the whereabouts of Chengzhi for a long time. This morning, I suddenly heard of his arrest and have urgently telegraphed the Shanghai Municipal Government to investigate. I will reply upon receiving a response and hope to hear from you soon. Wang Zhaoming."

Condolences from All Sides 130

Ms. He's relatives and friends and those who knew Liao Zhongkai during his lifetime rushed to Ms. He's residence yesterday after hearing the news to express their condolences in person. Madame Sun Yat-sen, Soong Ching-ling, also went to visit at about 3:00 yesterday afternoon and talked with Ms. He for a long time. Madame Sun is extremely committed to the work of protecting civil rights. It is said that she will make a considerable statement on the arrest of Liao Chengzhi.

Court Hearing 131

On the morning of the day before yesterday, Wang Qiliang from Shaoxing, Secretary-General of the All-China Federation of Trade Unions of the Communist Party, was active in the Gonghe Road area of Zhabei and was arrested by the inspectors of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Under interrogation, Wang admitted that he was an important member of the Communist Party and that he had arranged to hold a secret meeting with Luo Dunxian (also known as He Yongsheng), Yu Wenhua (also known as Lao Yu) from Henan, Liao Chengzhi from Guangdong, and others at Yu's residence at No. 9 Wufu Lane, Shanxi Road, at 2:00 that afternoon. The Public Security Bureau ordered a number of detectives to escort the suspect Wang and requested assistance from the Old Gate Police Station at 2:30 that afternoon. The head ordered Chinese detectives Wan Yuke and others to go to the address. Luo Dunxian, Yu Wenhua, and Liao Chengzhi were successively arrested in the east wing of the building upstairs. In addition, opium offenders Yuan Jingeng, Fan Gengsheng, and women You Qiusi and Yao Yinshi were also arrested and brought to the police station for investigation. Luo, Yu, and Liao all denied being communists. Liao Chengzhi also stated that he was the son of the martyr Liao Zhongkai and that his mother was He Xiangning, a current member of the Central Committee. He was born in Tokyo in 1908 and later studied at Tokyo Kosei Elementary School. He returned to China in 1927 and was admitted to the middle school of Lingnan University in Guangzhou. Later, he went to Japan to take the entrance exam for the Imperial University but failed. He then enrolled in Waseda University. After the "May 30th" incident, he returned to China on his mother's order. In 1928, he went to Germany and enrolled in the University of Halle-Wittenberg. He returned to China at the beginning of this year. He went to Shanxi Road to contact a tea merchant named Ouyang Chun on his mother's order to transport tea to the Northeast to comfort the anti-Japanese soldiers. He never knew what a communist was and had no political affiliations. Yesterday morning, the police station sent the opium offenders to the First Special District District Court for a judgment by Judge Feng, who sentenced Yuan Jingeng to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 60 yuan, Fan Zhensheng to one month of imprisonment, and You Qiusi to two months of imprisonment. The rest were acquitted. Luo, Yu, and Liao were transferred to the Criminal Division 1 of the Second Branch of the Higher Court. The police station was represented by Lawyer Gan Jingxian, and Liao Chengzhi was defended by Lawyer Wu Kaisheng. The Municipal Public Security Bureau was represented in court by legal counsel Lawyer Zhan Jifeng. At 10:00, the judge Yu Hua, along with judges Zhou Han and Jiang Shuzi and prosecutor Zhong Qing, took the bench and interrogated them. Lawyer Gan from the police station rose and stated the circumstances of the arrest of the defendants and requested that the defendants be temporarily detained for the sake of the defendants' interests and re-examined in a week. Fucai's representative then brought Wang Qiliang, who had been captured, to testify in the case. According to Wang, he joined the Communist Party in April last year, initially serving as a branch secretary and now serving as the Secretary-General of the All-China Federation of Trade Unions. The defendant Yu Wenhua is my secretary, Luo Dunxian is the secretary of the All-China Federation of Trade Unions Youth League, and Liao Chengzhi is the secretary of the Communist Party's Seafarers' Union, etc. The three defendants Luo, Yu, and Liao all denied ever joining the Communist Party or holding a position. Liao also stated that he had never met Wang Qiliang and that today was the first time he had ever met him. His statements are all unfounded. At this point, Lawyer Zhan of the Public Security Bureau rose and said that he had consulted with Liao's lawyer, and Lawyer Wu also agreed to transfer Liao to the Public Security Bureau. If the criminal acts cannot be proven, he can be released early to avoid innocent detention for a week. However, Liao heard this and stated that he had no proof of any crime and did not want to be transferred to any party or be detained by the police station. He only requested to be released unconditionally. Lawyer Wu then requested that bail be allowed during the adjourned period to allow him to go out and await summons. The police station lawyer stated that this case was a case of endangering the Republic of China and could be punished with the death penalty in accordance with the law. If bail could be granted, it would be impossible to investigate. Therefore, he expressed his opposition. Judge Yu then ordered all three defendants to be remanded in custody and re-examined on the afternoon of the 31st.

The Chaozhou-Shantou economy will be on the verge of bankruptcy. If we exhaust the resources, the consequences will be unimaginable. This matter concerns the people's livelihood and local security. In addition to sending separate telegrams, we urgently request that you report the situation and request an investigation and approval to order the abolition of the soybean cake tax secretly requested by the Shantou Taili Company and immediately telegraph to stop the company's harassment in order to maintain the original plan and save the people's lives. We cannot help but pray sincerely."

Surcharges for Meter Installation

Shanghai Water Company Releases Last Year's Business Report 139

Net Profit of One Million Three Hundred Forty-One Thousand and Seventy-Five Taels

Full-Year Dividends of 9% for Class A Shares, 7% for Class B Shares, and 8% for Class C Shares Can Be Issued

However, the Company Acknowledges That Users Who Do Not Waste Water May Receive Special Discounts

The Shanghai Water Company of the Public Concession released its business report for last year, stating that the income from users within the concession was 3,537,668 taels, and the surplus was 2,062,933 taels. Compared with the previous year's income of 3,579,496 taels and a surplus of 2,117,910 taels, both showed a slight decrease. After deducting various allocations from this surplus and adding half of the surplus from users outside the concession, the total net profit was 1,341,075 taels. After deducting the interim dividend of 484,116 taels, there was a remaining balance of 856,959 taels. It is now proposed to distribute an interim dividend of 35,000 taels, an annual bonus of 658,276 taels, and allocate 163,683 taels to the dividend reserve fund account. If this plan is approved by the shareholders' annual meeting on April 4, the total annual dividends will be 9% for Class A shares, 7% for Class B shares, and 8% for Class C shares. The net profit from users outside the concession and ships was 60,677 taels, a significant decrease compared to the previous year's net profit of 102,531 taels. This net profit, together with the balance carried over from the previous year, totaled 64,494 taels. It is now proposed to distribute 54,789 taels as dividends for Class A shares and 7,387 taels for Class B shares, with the remaining 2,318 taels carried over to the next year. Since the beginning of last year, water meters have been installed, and the installation is still ongoing. Once the water meters in each area are installed, fees will be calculated according to the water meter readings. However, when the fees calculated by the water meter are far higher than the fees previously calculated according to the rent, and the company also acknowledges that the user is not wasting water, a special discount may be granted with the approval of the Public Works Department. The company is currently negotiating with the Public Works Department to revise the water meter billing levels as a substitute for the special discount method. The company's land, according to the valuation of the Public Works Department, is worth 5,146,339 taels. Last year's expenses on buildings, water pipes, factories, and machinery totaled 1,276,587 taels. Last year, the total water sales volume increased by 0.00015, while the average daily sales volume decreased by 0.000125. Both the filtration plant and the pumping station are able to maintain good condition. The cost of pumping increased slightly compared to the previous year due to rising coal prices. The cost of water output decreased from 50.56 taels per million gallons in the previous year to 47.94 taels due to efforts to economize and the appreciation of the exchange rate. However, the total cost of tap water was 119.16 taels, compared to 116.11 taels in the previous year and 120.20 taels in 1930. The water meter installation project has now been completed in fourteen districts, with ten districts remaining. It is expected that all will be completed by July this year.

Competition Between American Oil and Russian Oil

Price Reduction by Both Companies 141

Opening of Longhua Temple 142

Longhua Temple, located in the southwest suburbs of this city, is a famous ancient temple in Shanghai. According to legend, it was built during the Chiwu period (238-251 AD) with hundreds of monks and nuns and covering more than one hundred acres of land. It flourished during the Qing Dynasty. The temple has a scripture library and a bronze Buddha from the Han Dynasty, with a seven-story pagoda nearby. When Qian Dajun was in charge of the Shanghai garrison, he chose the temple's western vegetable garden as a park and built a memorial tower for the fallen soldiers of the Thirty-second Army. Therefore, whenever the spring sunshine is bright and the peach blossoms are red and the willows are green, men and women in Shanghai, young and old, help each other and go to visit in an endless stream. However, after several wars, the doors and windows were damaged, the temples were dilapidated, and the monks and nuns were scattered. Last spring, the Xingxiu Hall was also destroyed by fire. Looking up at the Buddha's light, one cannot help but feel the vicissitudes of the past and present. The abbot of the temple, Yuanzhao, is familiar with the customary laws of the annual incense season and specially submitted a request to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to open the temple and provide proper protection during the incense season. It has now been approved and fully opened the day before yesterday. Liu Lun, the chief of the sixth district and third precinct of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, fearing that there would be too many visitors and that incidents could easily occur, temporarily added a squad of patrol police to maintain order on the spot. The weather was clear the day before yesterday, and the number of visitors from Jiangsu and Zhejiang was very crowded. The traffic on Longhua Road was heavy, and the scene was very lively.

Called by the Municipal Dock Business Office

Citywide Dock Foreman Discussion Meeting 143

On the morning of March 26th at 10:00 AM, the Dock Business Office convened a discussion meeting for dock foremen in the city at the auditorium on the third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. A total of one hundred and three people attended. Committee Member Zhang Jianbai presided over the meeting and reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating that the establishment of the office was just beginning, and internal organization would take some time, which is why the meeting was convened so late. It is regrettable that the leaders of each dock have not been able to meet sooner. The office has a major responsibility for the needs of the times, acting as a transitional period, in handling all matters between labor contractors and guiding the organization of labor unions. The foreman is the element closest to the workers. It is hoped that they will cooperate sincerely with the workers to increase the workers' interests and improve the status of the foremen, and so on. Then, Committee Member Zhang Xiaotong gave a speech, stating that he was extremely pleased to meet the leaders of the 90,000 dock workers in Shanghai today. He then put forward four points for the benefit of everyone: (1) The worker and the foreman are closely connected. Do not be incited or alienated by unscrupulous elements, causing conflict and falling into the trap of villains. (2) The office adopts peaceful means to resolve disputes between labor contractors and laborers through consultation, so that neither party suffers a loss. However, if a dispute does occur, you must come to the office and explain the situation honestly, so that there is no misunderstanding. (3) The situation in Northeast China is tense. Japanese imperialism is taking advantage of every opportunity and continuing its aggression. Foremen should pay special attention to the incitement of traitors. (4) Saving the country through aviation is the most important task at present. We should organize a committee and work hard to raise funds. It was then decided that the business office, the dock contractors, the foremen, and the workers would nominate responsible representatives to form an aviation fundraising committee. On the labor side, Wu Yaoting, Peng Desheng, Dong Boping, and Xu Jianye were immediately nominated as aviation fundraising committee members. The other aspects of dockhands and contractors will continue to nominate fundraising committee members.

Tobacco and Alcohol Industry

Proposed Establishment of a Provincial Joint Association 144

The nine trade associations of this city, including the tobacco exchange, sauce and wine, sauce garden, local yellow wine, sorghum liquor, restaurant, Shaoxing wine, Fen wine, and dry tobacco industries, have written to the tobacco and alcohol industry associations of Zhenjiang and ten other counties yesterday, seeking opinions on the proposal to reduce the burden of tobacco and alcohol taxes and requesting joint signatures to convene a joint meeting of representatives of the tobacco and alcohol industries of all counties in the province. The letter states: "Regarding the matter of tobacco and alcohol taxes, since the election of committee members was changed in the 21st year, there has been an increase in the proportion of taxes, which has increased the burden and caused disputes. Although mediation has been carried out to quell the disputes, our two industries have suffered deeply. Now that the year is about to expire, our associations are planning to discuss relief methods. The purpose is to make the national tax abundant and to avoid harassment of merchants, to seek a fundamental solution, and to make it a permanent solution. Recently, we have repeatedly received letters from the tobacco and alcohol industry associations of Suqian, Chongming, Yixing, and other counties to discuss the organization of a provincial joint association of the tobacco and alcohol industry. Our associations held the 13th joint meeting on the 27th of this month at the Tobacco Exchange Industry Association at No. 487 Ningbo Road. As the matter concerns the entire province, it is necessary to jointly convene several counties first in order to show prudence. It was decided to send letters to the tobacco and alcohol industry associations of Zhenjiang, Jiangning, Wuxian, Wuxi, Wujin, Changshu, Wujiang, Taixing, Nantong, Taixian, and ten other counties with large tax ratios to seek opinions. After receiving replies, a date will be set to jointly sign and send letters to the tobacco and alcohol industry associations of all counties in the province, nominating responsible representatives to organize a provincial joint association of the tobacco and alcohol industry to jointly discuss and improve methods, so as to relieve suffering and permanently eliminate disputes. This has been unanimously approved. In addition to sending separate letters, this special letter is to inform you. We hope that your association will consider this matter and, if you agree, please reply within one week so that we can determine the date and jointly send a letter to convene a meeting of all counties in order to achieve unity and show prudence. We will be very grateful."

Collection of Thirty Cents (Mexican Dollars) Per Hundred Jin

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, Public Security Bureau, Finance Bureau, and Health Bureau jointly announced: "Regarding the matter of inspection of meat products entering the city, the implementation has been temporarily postponed due to the issue of jurisdiction, which is still awaiting instructions. The Health Bureau has now received Instruction No. 4816 from the Municipal Government and an Instruction from the Executive Yuan that the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, according to the city government's approved regulations on the inspection of meat products entering the city, will conduct inspections of cured hams and other meat products. It is reported by the city government that the purpose is to crack down on the entry of diseased meat and protect public health. Before the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has established regulations for the domestic sales inspection of goods, it should be temporarily approved to operate in accordance with these regulations. Once the regulations of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce are established and implemented, they should be handled in accordance with the regulations of the ministry to avoid conflicts with the central administrative authority. In addition to notifying the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the city government is hereby ordered to comply with this order and report accordingly. In accordance with this, our bureau has jointly decided to implement the inspection on April 1st, 22nd year of the Republic of China, and to change the inspection fee to only 30 cents (Mexican dollars) per hundred jin, which has been reported to the city government for record. According to the provisions of Article 7 of the regulations, anyone carrying more than one hundred jin of meat products into the city must first purchase a meat product inspection certificate at any tax collection office of the Finance Bureau in order to obtain a certificate for inspection, otherwise they will be punished according to the regulations. If there are any unscrupulous elements who deliberately confuse and attempt to obstruct, they will be seriously investigated and dealt with. In addition to ordering subordinates to investigate at any time, this announcement is hereby made known to all. This announcement is made on the 3rd month of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. Director of the Bureau of Social Affairs Wu Xingya, Director of the Bureau of Public Security Wen Hongen, Director of the Bureau of Finance Cai Zengji, Director of the Bureau of Health Li Ting'an."

Water Cut Off in Weishui Lane and Other Areas

Water Company Has Sent Plumbers to Restore Water Supply 147

Payment Method Still Under Discussion

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that since the British-owned Shanghai Water Company of the Public Concession installed new water meters in the homes within the concession, water prices have suddenly increased several times, even exceeding the rent, which has caused opposition from all walks of life. The landlords, feeling the pinch, have stopped paying water bills. Although various parties have mediated, the difference is too great to be reconciled. The water company, wanting to enforce its authority, forcibly cut off water to the areas with the most water consumption, which provoked resistance from residents. All parties believe that this stalemate is not appropriate and have requested relevant parties to vigorously mediate with the water company and the Public Works Department, and to hold subcommittee meetings to study ways to resolve the water bill dispute. The water company proposed a temporary compromise, that the water bills owed before the end of February be paid in full at 10% of the rent, and that the water pipes cut off by the water company be restored by the company's plumbers. The property owners' association held a temporary members' meeting to discuss the matter. It was generally believed that this method was not satisfactory. However, in order to take care of the convenience of residents, it was temporarily handled according to the above method, but the company was required to restore the water pipes first, and then pay the fees, which could be guaranteed by the Chinese directors. It was not convenient to acknowledge the new payment method starting from March. According to news from the property owners' association, the water company has sent plumbers to restore water to Weishui Lane, Yuanfang Road, Jingyu Lane, and more than ten other areas where water was cut off, and drinking water has been supplied as usual. However, Sanshin Lane on Tangshan Road and Shuncheng Lane on Yangshupu Road have not yet been opened because the owners of Sanshin Lane have not yet contacted the property owners' association, so the water is still cut off. Shuncheng Lane has no need for tap water because it has drilled an artesian well. According to the person in charge of the association, if the water cut off areas want to restore the usual supply of remaining materials, they can contact the association immediately for similar handling. As for the new payment method starting from March, there is no concrete method yet, and the relevant parties are still discussing it. In short, the water bill must be based on the principle that the owner can afford it, so that both parties can reach a fair solution.

Singapore

Postage for Letters Has Not Increased 151

Slight increase for private postal services

Completely unrelated to the public

The "Zi Lin" newspaper reported that Reuters Singapore reported yesterday that the local Chinese in that port were protesting against the Chinese postal authorities' intention to increase the postage for letters from private postal services to one corner and two and a half points. The reporter inquired with the Shanghai Postal Administration and learned that the Chinese postal authorities still allow private postal services in Guangzhou, Shantou, Xiamen, and other places to collect and send mail to Singapore and other ports with a larger number of overseas Chinese through the post office. However, for letters to other ports, the international postage rate of 2.5 jiao per letter is charged. Only in Singapore is the fee reduced by half for letters handled by private postal services. In the past, when the postage for foreign letters was 1 jiao, letters sent to Singapore by private postal services enjoyed a special right to deduct 5 fen. Later, when the postage for foreign letters increased to 2.5 jiao, this postage should have automatically increased to 1 jiao and 2.5 fen, but in order to be considerate of the merchants' difficulties, it was delayed. Therefore, to this day, letters sent to Singapore by private postal services still pay 5 fen. Conversely, letters sent from Singapore to China have been charged 8 Singapore cents per letter since October of last year, equivalent to 1 jiao and 6 fen in national currency. Therefore, the proposed increase this time is only for the postage paid by private postal services and is unrelated to the public. It will still maintain the right to a half reduction and is lighter than the postage for mail from Singapore to China.

Former Songhu Police Department

Dispute Over Loan Owed to Guangdong Bank 153

Loan Delayed for a Long Time and Not Repaid

Guarantors Xu Qianlin and Others Sued

Shanghai gentry and merchants Xu Qianlin and Wang Binyan were recently sued by lawyer Yan, representing Guangdong Bank, in the First Special District District Court for defaulting on a loan. It is alleged that the defendants borrowed 5,000 Shanghai taels from the bank on April 20th of the Republic of China Year 14, with an agreement to repay the loan three months later. The interest was calculated at a rate of 10 taels per 100 taels per annum. Accumulating until the previous month, the outstanding interest had reached 7,506 taels and 8 qian. Combining the principal and interest, the total debt was 12,506 taels and 8 qian. Despite repeated reminders, the defendants have been making excuses for delay. Therefore, the lawsuit was filed, requesting a judgment ordering the full repayment of the principal and interest. After being sued, Xu and others also hired lawyer Zhao Chuanding to file a defense, stating that at the time of the loan, the provincial treasury was empty after the Qi-Lu war, and the Songhu police salaries were in default, endangering local security. The former Magistrate Li of Shanghai County and the former Director Chang of the Songhu Police Department raised funds from the Chamber of Commerce. Chen Bingqian introduced the Police Department to borrow 5,000 taels of silver from Guangdong Bank, and the two defendants were asked to act as guarantors. A promissory note was written and given to the bank. The note clearly stated that the defendants were only guarantors and that there was an agreement to repay the loan. This can be verified by records in the municipal government and the Public Security Bureau, and is also evidenced by the plaintiff's letters. Now, the plaintiff's claim in the lawsuit that the defendants borrowed the money is a lie. Although the debt has not been repaid, the principal debtor is actually the Municipal Public Security Bureau. On February 16th of this year, the plaintiff commissioned lawyer Mi to write a letter requesting the defendants to fulfill their guarantee obligations. The defendants explained that since the Municipal Public Security Bureau had succeeded the Police Department in inheriting the debt, the plaintiff's claim should be made against the Municipal Public Security Bureau. It is unreasonable to abandon the principal debtor and directly demand payment from the defendants, who are only guarantors. Later, the plaintiff's lawyer wrote again, stating that the municipal government seemed unwilling to take responsibility, so the defendants were asked to repay on their behalf. The defendants checked the Public Security Bureau's letter, which clearly instructed the plaintiff on how to seek payment and did not indicate any intention to default. The plaintiff insisted that the Municipal Public Security Bureau was evading responsibility, which was close to insulting the administrative authorities and was truly unreasonable. Now, the plaintiff has listed the defendants as defendants, accusing them of borrowing money and failing to repay, and has directly filed a lawsuit. According to the law, the liability of a guarantor is subordinate and clearly stipulates that the guarantor shall perform the obligation on behalf of the principal debtor if the principal debtor fails to perform the obligation. This is the first characteristic of a guarantee debt. There is also a supplementary nature, that is, to supplement the performance of the principal debt, and the performance of the principal debtor should be the priority. The creditor is not allowed to request performance directly from the guarantor before the principal debtor. This is the second characteristic of a guarantee debt. Therefore, the guarantor has the right to demand investigation and the right to prior litigation. In this case, the principal debtor is the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the defendants are only guarantors, which is an indisputable fact. The Municipal Public Security Bureau has neither denied the debt nor expressed any intention of not performing it. It has also stated that the matter is real and has been submitted to the higher authorities for verification. The reason for the non-payment is simply that no instructions have been received. This is an administrative procedure. How can it be said that the city is deliberately evading responsibility? The plaintiff did not quietly await the disposition of the municipal government, nor did it apply to the municipal government as instructed by the Public Security Bureau. Instead, it insulted the authorities, making wild claims that the Municipal Public Security Bureau was deliberately evading responsibility and unwilling to take responsibility. It has directly filed a lawsuit against the defendants before the principal debtor. According to the law, there is no reason for this. It is requested that the plaintiff's lawsuit be dismissed. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Peng held a hearing. Because the facts of the loan were not disputed, the hearing was concluded immediately after the examination. However, the two sides had different opinions on the issue of responsibility. The lawyers on both sides debated this point for a long time. After the two sides concluded their arguments, Judge Yang ordered that a date be set for the verdict.

How Is This Behavior Different from That of Beasts?

Wang Monk, a local extra actor in the Xianshi Amusement Park Grand Theater on Jing Road, has always been vulgar, committing crimes and offenses more than once. Although he has been punished, he has not repented. Abusing young children is his most prominent crime. Previously, Sun Yunyu, a 16-year-old boy from Suzhou, originally worked on a ship. At the end of last year, he lost his job for some reason and was stranded in Shanghai. In January of this year, Wang saw him passing through the Hongkou area. Because he was young and easy to deceive, Wang used enticement. The boy had no money to return home, so he spent his days with Wang. Wang pretended to be his apprentice and spent the nights with him. From then on, he was forcibly sodomized every night. The boy suffered greatly and tried to escape twice, but Wang had many followers and many eyes and ears. He was always found and returned, and the surveillance was even stricter. The boy believed him. Wang then took him to a bathhouse, had him wash his whole body, and took him to the Xinyuelai Inn on Wuhu Road at night. He did to Yang what he had done to Sun, also pretending to be his apprentice, and taught him various slang terms popular in the underworld. The boy could not bear the abuse and wanted to escape, but there was no opportunity. Five days ago, Wang took Sun out, resulting in a lapse in security. Yang finally escaped from the tiger's mouth and was found by a detective, who took him to the Laozha Police Station and transferred him to the hospital. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Special District District Court. Presiding Judge Feng Shide held a hearing. Police lawyer Ru Baozhen stated that the case was related to public morals and requested that the hearing be closed to the public. The court approved the request. Then, he stated the various obscene acts committed by the defendant in abusing the boys and requested that the defendant be severely punished. Finally, he stated that Sun had not yet been examined by a doctor and requested that the case be adjourned for further investigation. Then, Yang and Sun testified in turn about the abuse they had suffered. When Wang Monk was questioned, he only admitted to taking the two boys as apprentices and denied everything else. Judge Feng then ordered the defendant to be detained. Yang and Sun were temporarily sent to the Women and Children's Relief Association. The case was adjourned for seven days for further investigation.

Poyang Wheel Collides with a Liquor Boat 157

丨Boat Crew Members Drift Away with the Waves丨

The Tongyihe Liquor Boat from South City was sailing from north to south after loading liquor cargo at the Sampan Factory at 3:00 AM yesterday morning. When passing the Taikoo Wharf, the company's Poyang Wheel left the port and sailed north without sounding its horn, proceeding northward. The liquor boat was unable to avoid it in time and was overturned by the wheel. The liquor it was carrying was completely poured into the Huangpu River. Of the three crew members, only two were rescued. One of them, Zhu Er, was swept away by the waves and died. The firm and the families of the boat owner and crew members believe that the Poyang Wheel neglected its duties, resulting in a major loss of life and cargo. They have reported the facts to the Jianghai Customs Water Patrol Team, requesting a fair investigation, and have also sent letters to fellow villagers' associations in Pudong and Shaoxing, requesting assistance.

Pan Xiangsen and Ji Zhongren

Accusation of Embezzling Inheritance 158

丨Hiding the Property Ledger丨

Chai Yanxu, son of the deceased Suzhou tycoon Chai Bingsheng, was entrusted by his relatives Pan Xiangsen and Ji Zhongren to keep a large number of precious ornaments left by his late mother for thirteen years. He repeatedly demanded their return without success. As a last resort, he hired lawyers Jiang Yiping, Qin Liankui, and Yang Zhihao to file a criminal complaint in the First Special Court, accusing them of embezzlement, etc. After repeated hearings, the court ordered Lou Mingshi, an important witness for the defendants, to appear in court for further questioning. Yesterday (the 28th) afternoon, Judge Zhan Liangce continued the hearing. The witness summoned for the plaintiff appeared, but none of the defendants appeared for various reasons. The plaintiff, Chai Yanxu, stated that the ornaments were deposited by the defendants in their personal names in the safe deposit box of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank. All transactions were handled by the defendants. On February 4th of the 14th year, he and his wife accompanied Pan Disheng, son of Pan Xiangsen, to the bank to retrieve the items. At that time, a property ledger was found. They took this ledger to the Hainemann's foreign firm to consult with his brother-in-law, Wu Langxi. Wu copied a list from the ledger. Then, Pan Disheng wrote the words "Di Dui" (checked by Di) on the ledger. The original ledger was still taken away by Pan Disheng. Later, Wu transcribed the list into another ledger. He only needs to ask the defendants to hand over the original ledger and ask Zhao Jieting to testify that Mr. and Mrs. Chai and Pan Disheng visited Wu Langxi at Hainemann's firm. Because Pan and Chai were arguing, Wu advised them and copied a list from the ledger, and the original ledger was taken away by Pan. According to Chai's statement, a small part of the ornaments deposited by the defendants was retrieved on the 25th day of the twelfth lunar month in the Bingyin year, but the majority of them have not been returned despite repeated requests. When questioned, the defendant Pan Xiangsen firmly stated that all the ornaments had been returned in full. At that time, only a list of ornaments was recorded, and there was no so-called ledger. After further questioning, Pan Xiangsen claimed to have sold 2,000 taels of pearls and 100 yuan. Because the important witness Lou Mingshi (the person who wrote the original property ledger) arrived, the wives of Pan Xiangsen and Zhang Zhenhou were summoned for questioning. Therefore, the hearing was adjourned to April 11th for further investigation.

Old Baidu, Pudong

Fire at Yifengxiang Hotel 159

The Yifengxiang Hotel at No. 57, the street behind the Tongchun Inn in Old Baidu, Pudong, suddenly caught fire at 1:00 AM yesterday morning. Because it was midnight, no one noticed it for a while. The owner, Li Qing, was awakened in his sleep and urgently woke up his family and staff, and they all escaped through the back door, avoiding disaster. Before long, the fire broke through the roof. A nearby guard noticed it and urgently sounded an alarm whistle for assistance. The surrounding neighbors were all awakened and fled outwards. The fire became more and more intense and soon spread to the double-frontage Tongxin Chang Cigarette and Paper Shop at Nos. 59 and 61 next door. The shop was full of flammable items such as paper, candles, and kerosene, so the flames were fueled and became even more intense. The Tongchun Fu's private fire engine was driven out to draw water for firefighting. Because the fire was raging, it was difficult to extinguish it for a while. By 3:00 AM, it had also destroyed a tiger stove before gradually being extinguished. However, the embers inside the fire site were still smoldering until dawn. When the fire was raging, Yang Zhongquan, the director of the Third District First Branch, and Inspector Sun led the police to maintain order around the fire site, so no incidents occurred. Afterwards, the fire station took the hotel owner Li Fuqing, a native of Suqian, and the Tongxin Chang shop owner Mingchang, a native of Ningbo (insured), along with the witness Zhang Atao, to the station for separate interrogation. It was decided to send Li and Chen to the headquarters for further investigation. The witness Zhang Atao was temporarily released on bail pending summons.

British Soldier's Vehicle Crushes a Chinese Child to Death 160

At around 9:00 AM yesterday morning, at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Baker Road in the Public Concession, a nearby child named Zhu Deyuan, nine years old, was wandering in the road. He suddenly tried to cross the road. A British military vehicle, identified as No. 9888, was coming towards him. He was unable to avoid it in time and was knocked to the ground, breaking his ribs and injuring his head. He was on the verge of death. After hearing the news, Chinese police officer No. 732 rushed to the scene, recorded the vehicle number, and immediately sent the injured child to Renji Hospital. Due to the severity of his injuries, he died at 6:15 PM.

Endless Illegal Gambling Syndicates 161

Double Gold Company Busted

The major illegal gambling syndicates in this city, originally divided into North and South factories, were merged into one factory on March 1st of this year. As a result, the gambling outlets in the lanes of both the Chinese and foreign concessions are visible everywhere. Gambling is even more prevalent than before. Three rounds are run per day. Each round brings in around 40,000 to 50,000 yuan for the major factories. Every day at 2:00 PM, 7:30 PM, and 2:00 AM in the middle of the night, the report-carrying bicycles (called "fast horses" by these people) on the various roads are constantly on the move. A person named Shuangqing has more than ten gambling outlets in the Baoyu Lane and Xinchang Lane of the French Concession. He has considerable power among the gambling gangs. The gambling outlet's signboard is the Double Gold Company, divided into East, West, North, and South. Each outlet brings in thousands of yuan. At around 7:00 PM yesterday evening, the head of the Da Zi Ming Zhong Police Station in the French Concession sent more than ten Chinese and French detectives, including Vietnamese police officers, to secretly raid the Double Gold Company gambling outlet at No. 41 Baoyu Lane. At that time, gamblers were gathered there, and more than ten people were arrested, along with three wooden boxes of gambling slips. They were taken to the police station and reported to the head of the police for verification.

A Kidnapping Case Was Uncovered on the Yushun Steamer 162

Each Child's Testimony Confirmed, Kidnappers Also Sixteen or Seventeen Years Old

The China Merchants Bureau's Yushun Steamer, which travels between Fuzhou, Xiamen, and other ports, left its berth in Shanghai at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. Prior to this, Qiao Songren, the South Wharf Patrol Chief of the Bureau, inspected the ship at around 2:00 PM. While inspecting the large cabin, he heard the sounds of children. He immediately conducted a search and found four kidnapped boys and one kidnapper in the large cabin. He immediately inquired about them in secret. There were two accomplices in the passenger cabin. He immediately took the arrested kidnapper to identify and capture them. All three kidnappers were arrested without a single one escaping. Patrol Chief Qiao then interrogated them separately. According to Gu Yongzhen, the eldest of the kidnapped boys, 17 years old and from Hangzhou, he was kidnapped by the kidnapper Chen Afa (the one currently arrested) at the age of 13 and sold to the Fuda Automobile Company. Because he had suffered for many years and had no money, he finally escaped to Shanghai this year. Unexpectedly, he met Chen Afa on Fourth Horse Road and was dragged back again. This is the second time he has been kidnapped. According to the boy Weng Xiaomao, 14 years old and from Hangzhou, he was kidnapped by Wang Jinqing and Chen Afa on Fourth Horse Road and did not know where he was being taken. According to the boy Yang Axiang, from Hangzhou, 13 years old, he lived in Caoqiaomen. According to the boy Yao Abao, from Suzhou, his father's name was A Qiao, a tailor. He was kidnapped by Wang Jinfa at the entrance of the Great World while making clothes in Mingde Lane in the British Concession. According to the kidnapper Wang Jinfa, 17 years old and from Nanjing, he planted flowers in the Zhongshan Garden in Xiamen. He had done it once before. In November of last year, Chen Afa kidnapped a boy, 15 years old, on Minguo Road and took him to Guangdong. According to the kidnapper Chen Afa, he made toothpaste in Pudong. The kidnapper Wang Chunfa, 16 years old and from Hangzhou, gave cunning statements. Patrol Chief Qiao, with solid evidence, immediately escorted all the people and witnesses to the Water Patrol Police Station to be sent to court for severe punishment.

Rickshaw Puller Killed by Car 163

On the morning of December 16th of last year, at 8:30 AM, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters sent driver Chen Yongde to drive car No. 6157 to Rongren Lane on Xujiahui Road in the French Concession, Xieqiao, to pick up an official to go to the headquarters to work. When Chen's car turned around at the entrance of Rongren Lane, its head collided with Yu Jiaming, a rickshaw puller from Haimen, who was parked on the side of the road, causing injuries to his head, waist, left leg, and other places. He fell to the ground. A police officer recorded the number and reported it to the police station. The injured person was sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment, but he did not recover. Yu's wife, Gu, filed a criminal complaint in the Second Special Court, accusing the driver Chen Yongde of causing injury. The case had not yet been concluded when Yu died in the hospital due to the severity of his injuries. The hospital notified the police station's vehicle department to send the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home for an autopsy. Yesterday, the Second Special Court requested Prosecutor Deng to come to the funeral home to confirm that the deceased had died from injuries sustained in a car accident. The body was ordered to be claimed by the family. The defendant was sent to the case by the vehicle department for interrogation.

Relocation of Mathematics Expert Guan Liushu 165

Mr. Guan Liushu, also known as Dunsou, served as a Prefect in the Qing Dynasty after serving as an Imperial Academy Compiler. He is deeply versed in the "Book of Changes" and is proficient in mathematics, numerology, and feng shui. In recent years, he has resided in Shanghai, providing divination and residential consultations, all of which have proven remarkably accurate. Mr. Guan originally resided in Kangli, Avenue Joffre. However, due to the large number of visitors seeking his guidance each day, the original residence could not accommodate them. Letter to the Editor 167

To the Editor:

Back in July of the 12th year of the Republic of China [1923], when I was working as a section chief at the Jiangsu Bureau of Foreign Affairs, 160 yuan was deducted from my salary as part of a fund to redeem the Jiaoji Railway. The negotiator, Mr. Xu, sent the sum to the Songhu Military Governor's Office for storage. Subsequently, a letter was received from the Military Governor proposing that the funds be used to purchase government bonds, to be deposited in the Yanyeh, Dalu, and Jitong banks, with interest at 8% every six months, pending central government negotiations and the announcement of concrete measures to exchange for Jiaoji Railway shares. I have a receipt with the Foreign Affairs Bureau's third seal as proof. Ten years have passed, and there has been no announcement as to whether this sum has been used to redeem the railway or remains deposited in the bank. Having read in the newspaper that the former Songhu Military Governor, He Fenglin, is in Shanghai raising funds for the World Red Cross Society, I yesterday sent a letter to the Shanghai Office of the World Red Cross Society, offering to donate the deducted 160 yuan in full to the society, requesting that they contact Mr. He. Considering that dozens of colleagues from the former Foreign Affairs Bureau had salary deductions, amounting to a significant sum, I propose that all colleagues donate these funds to the Red Cross Society or the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army Support Association, to prevent public funds from being lost. I hope this sentiment can be shared. As colleagues are scattered in all directions, it is difficult to convene a meeting to discuss. I respectfully request that your publication, recognizing the good cause involved, publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" column so that everyone may be informed. Thank you.

Respectfully,

Shang Shengbo, March 26th.

To the Editor:

Having read in your newspaper on the 29th of this month the news regarding the laid-off employees of the two railways petitioning the Party and government authorities, the three demands listed are accurate. However, regarding the statement that "since Huang Boqiao took office, he has strived to reorganize, repay foreign debts, and drastically reduce redundant staff," this does not align with the facts. We do not know what your newspaper's basis for this is: (1) Since Mr. Huang took office, there has been no reorganization; (2) The repayment of foreign debt is the implementation of a previous plan from October 1st of last year, where 10% of daily revenue is deposited into HSBC, to be allocated when a sufficient amount is accumulated; this was handled by the previous administration; (3) The staff and officers of all levels laid off by Mr. Huang this time all had actual work and were not redundant staff. Currently, we and our colleagues are in discussions with Mr. Huang based on the facts. We especially request that you publish this correction in the "Letters to the Editor" column so that society may understand the truth and avoid misunderstandings. We earnestly hope for this.

Respectfully,

The Laid-Off Employees of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, March 29th.

Calligraphy and Painting 169

Calligraphers and Painters Waive Fees Due to National Crisis: Calligraphers Fu Pu'an (seal script) and Pu Ting (regular script), in light of the ongoing national crisis and their inability to express themselves fully, believing that pearls are insufficient to revitalize the people's spirit, have specially engraved stamps bearing the inscription "Restore the Lost Territories," which they affix to their works to express their heartfelt grief over the national crisis. They will not accept fees for their work, only for paper and ink costs. Regardless of size, scrolls, panels, and screens within four feet will cost six dimes per piece, within six feet will cost one yuan per piece, and within eight feet will cost three yuan per piece. This will continue until the lost territories are recovered. They also invite all members of the National Essence Calligraphy and Painting Society at 38 Wangyun Road, Hongqiao, to participate: He Bomin, Zhang Feixiong, Zhang Yanmou, Wu Jiren, calligraphers Qian Zong'an, Juanyou Jushi, Hu Jun, Lü Ying, and painters of figures, landscapes, antiques, birds and animals, ink dragons, and portraits. They will all participate, charging only 30% of their original fees to cover paper, brush, and ink costs. Fee schedules can be requested by mail.

Reader Advisory 174

Discussion on Women's Issues 175

| Letter from Zhu Yingjun of Shanghai |

I have read Mr. Wang Muchong's letter of the 13th. He says his wife "cannot read, does not understand human relationships, and is ignorant of world affairs." In a nutshell, he is saying that his wife has no knowledge. Here I want to ask: What is knowledge? Is reading tens of thousands of books and obtaining a doctorate degree while being someone who does not work to eat considered knowledge? Conversely, even if one cannot read and does not have a doctorate or bachelor's degree, but does work that benefits the group every day, at least not being a parasite on society, is this considered true knowledge? Having clarified this point, I will discuss Mr. Wang's wife. Mr. Wang's wife is clearly what people call an old-fashioned woman. However, old-fashioned women can cook, wash clothes, help with all household tasks, and raise children, allowing their husbands to focus on the work they should be doing. Is this beneficial to society? Naturally, I am not saying that women should only do these things, but in any case, it is ten thousand times better than those modern women who only care about applying makeup, going to the movies, and going to dance halls. Although there are some women with true knowledge, in the current China, "heroes have no place to use their talents," and knowledge is merely an ornament for them, while in reality, they are nothing more than parasites on society. It is better to be like Mr. Wang's wife, who, although she does not have much knowledge (according to Mr. Wang's view), can do some practical work for society little by little. Furthermore, Mr. Wang says: "Originally, my family was not very well-off, but her family is rich." He also says: "Her temperament is very gentle, she is very humble and modest towards me, and not arrogant..." From this, it seems that Mr. Wang's wife is a woman of very good character. Although she comes from a wealthy family, she has the awareness of those who are not wealthy. If properly trained, it would not be difficult for her to become a vanguard in reforming society. In fact, there are already many women like this. Mr. Wang is probably a college student. College students have a responsibility to reform society. You must know that in order to reform society, you must first sacrifice yourself and at the same time uplift the weak in society. Even if Mr. Wang considers his marriage unsatisfactory, he must act based on this principle. In other words, it is acceptable to tolerate one's wife having little knowledge, while at the same time diligently teaching her to gain knowledge. This is the correct way. Otherwise, how can you brag and say, "I will do things for society in the future, I am an outstanding member of society," if it is not just empty talk!

This letter is only a supplement from the reporter.

Editor's Note: Regarding Mr. Wang Muchong's letter, this column has already provided a detailed response (see the 13th issue of this column). Now that we have received Mr. Zhu's letter, which supplements what the reporter's response lacked, we are publishing it above.

Issues of Opening a Store and Borrowing Money 176

| Letter from Qu Wenshou of Shanghai |

Editor: Every day I read the "Reader Advisory" section, which answers readers' common questions from a scientific and materialist standpoint. I sincerely and courageously appreciate and accept them. Therefore, my addiction to reading your column is more important and emphasized than reading the news or literary columns in the entire newspaper! For this reason, in the Chinese language test for the news correspondence school run by your newspaper, in the essay question "Criticism and suggestions for this newspaper," I especially praised your column and criticized it, but I have not received a response. Now, I am raising two important and serious questions in the title above. Please disclose them in your newspaper! The first question is about the following: Through the introduction of relatives and friends, I entered this store as a worker selling goods and keeping accounts. It has only been eight months, but the hierarchy is very strict, especially the so-called proprietress, who is like a supervisory committee member and the most vicious woman's heart. The proprietress handles and monitors the store's trivial matters. Every day, the boss treats the employees with a stern face, which, as those who have experienced such an environment know, is no less severe than a judge treating a prisoner. The young master and the proprietress are no exception. In our ×× store, a so-called husband-and-wife shop, I live and work under their constant ridicule. Therefore, the mutual antipathy has been built up so high that it seems to resemble a pyramid, as deep as a flowing spring! For this reason, we are now gathering several colleagues from the store, preparing to leave this cage, and gathering shares to start our own new store in Shanghai, the same type of business. In business, we will inevitably be envied by the old boss who is about to be abandoned. Currently, we (the colleagues) are preparing to resign from the boss en masse. Does this, if the boss deems me as the initiator, involve legal issues? The second question is a question that arises from the first question: Borrowing money. In Shanghai, I have a wealthy relative who owns dozens of city houses, and I collect rent for him. In the past, because some of our fellow villagers borrowed money from him and did not repay it, he views my credit (borrowing money) as being of the same kind. It is difficult to get his approval to borrow. So, now that I am collecting rent for him and handling more than a thousand yuan in cash every month, I am thinking of secretly appropriating three hundred yuan from the rent money (as start-up capital for the store) when he does not allow me to borrow in person. Then, I will tell him about it as a plan for forced borrowing. At this time, the relationship between the two parties will be broken, but what about the legal issues?

Answer: You previously "especially praised and criticized this column" in the essay for the recruitment examination for the news correspondence school run by this newspaper. We are truly ashamed to hear this praise, because our colleagues have limited knowledge and cultivation, and we are always afraid that we will not be able to meet the earnest expectations of the readers. We sincerely accept this criticism. To what extent the readers' criticism is genuine also shows to what extent our small efforts have gained the attention of the readers. Moreover, we not only want to be advisors to the readers, but also hope that readers will provide us with real materials from social life. This is a digression. Now, let us answer the two questions you raised as follows: If you and your colleagues form a new store together, if the procedures are clear and the separation is proper, it may not involve legal issues. But this does not mean that your boss will not sabotage it. Sabotage is of course unavoidable, but as long as your group is solid, it will not matter. However, I think there is a bit of self-contradiction in your matter. You yourselves have awakened to the conflict of interests due to the abuse of the old boss and the proprietress, but you must know that the relationship of conflict of interests is formed by the entire social organization and the entire economic system. To solve this problem, you must think from the perspective of the entire society and start with a great mass organization to have a solution. If everyone leaves the old boss's power and becomes the boss themselves, in this old-fashioned society, if you become the boss, what method will you use not to be harsh on people? Do you have any ideal plans? May I ask? This is the first question. You can borrow money from people, but if you "secretly appropriate" and "forcefully borrow," it can easily affect the feelings of both parties, or even lead to legal problems, or even fatally damage your newly opened business. In our opinion, there is something wrong with what you are doing. If you insist on doing it your own way, you will definitely fail. Be careful! This is the second question.

Student Unrest in Northern Anhui May Be Resolved 178

Ministry of Education Sends Personnel to Investigate and Handle

(Anhui News) The Anhui Education Department's merger of four vocational schools, relocation of two normal schools, and replacement of the principals of four or five schools in northern Anhui have caused disputes that have yet to be resolved. The Education Department has now decided not to relocate the two normal schools for the time being, but the drive to oust the principal at the Seventh Vocational School remains unresolved. Various parties have criticized the Education Department, and the Provincial Party Headquarters has sent a letter to the Provincial Government, instructing the Education Department to handle the matter carefully. The Education Department, due to the situation, sent Section Chief Wu Zhongxian to Beijing to report to the Ministry of Education, requesting a solution. The Ministry of Education has sent Section Chief Dai Yingguan to Bengbu on the 27th to investigate and handle the matter. The student unrest in northern Anhui may be resolved as a result. Principal Ling Xiaofen of the newly appointed Second Normal School has not yet taken office. Whether there will be other problems after the Seventh Vocational School issue is resolved remains to be seen.

Recent News on Inspection of Anhui Education

The Ministry of Education previously sent Guo Xincong, Chen Kezhong, and Tang Xifen to inspect Anhui Provincial University and general education. The inspectors have returned to Beijing one after another. The inspection reports are currently being compiled jointly. It is reported that Guo and Chen inspected Anhui University, the Anqing Provincial Women's Middle School, the Provincial First Middle School, three vocational schools, and the Provincial Library. In addition to the men's and women's middle schools and vocational schools in Anqing, they also inspected primary and secondary schools in other locations. When inspecting the university and the schools in the provincial capital, Education Commissioner Zhu Tinghu accompanied them. The Anhui University campus is rented, with monthly rent payments of several hundred yuan. The university has identified a new campus with a large area, but due to the national crisis, construction funds have not yet been received, so construction has not begun. The university is divided into the Colleges of Arts, Sciences, and Law, with a larger number of law students. Each department has a large number of professors, and the facilities are good. Teachers' salaries are paid in full, while staff salaries are paid at 80%. The middle schools and vocational schools are operating with good spirit and have decent facilities. The library's collection is mainly Chinese books, with a slight lack of books for specialized academic research.

Reception Report: The Jiaotong University Industrial and Railway Exhibition reception for the city's press was attended by more than 40 reporters from Chinese and foreign newspapers. First, Xu Mingcai, the director of publicity for the exhibition, reported, briefly stating: The university's Industrial and Railway Exhibition is now ready. We have specially invited the press to visit. We are very pleased that you have graciously come. We hope you will not hesitate to offer your guidance so that we can improve. There are about three points regarding today's reception, which I will briefly report: (1) Running a school and running a news organization share the responsibility of educating society and are closely related. However, due to the heavy workload of education, there are few opportunities to interact. We are taking advantage of the opening of the exhibition to meet with you, and we will work even harder together in the future. (2) Exhibitions are held dozens of times a year in major cities in Europe and the United States. The purpose is to make the public interested in industrial construction and then engage in research and invention. When the university celebrated its 30th anniversary, it also held an exhibition. At that time, few domestic manufacturers participated, but the purpose was also to make the Chinese people aware of the situation of industrial and railway construction and arouse their interest. This time, more domestic factories are participating, and it can also be used to introduce the achievements of the Chinese people's efforts in industry over the past seven years. (3) All the preparations and arrangements for this exhibition were done in spare time. Due to the short time, there may be some imperfections, so we have invited you to come and visit first, hoping to receive your guidance. Then, President Li Zhaohuan reported on the significance of holding the Industrial and Railway Exhibition, briefly stating: China has been oppressed by the great powers in recent years and has advocated resistance, but because there has been little preparation, it has ultimately failed. The university also held an exhibition seven years ago, which mostly displayed foreign products. Outsiders did not understand and thought it was promoting foreign goods and advertising for foreign businesses. In fact, China's lack of preparation lies in the backwardness of its industry, and the underdevelopment of industry lies in the fact that the Chinese people are not interested in industry. Therefore, the significance of the exhibition is to make the Chinese people aware of industrial construction, and various discussion sessions will be held, but they will not be publicized because they are related to national defense.

Exhibition Participants: The deadline for Chinese and foreign manufacturers participating in the exhibition was last night. There are more than 230 in total. (1) Industrial Exhibition: The machines on display include those from Laina Printing Machinery Manufacturing Factory, Xintong Trading Company, Kailuo Mining Bureau, Zhendan Iron Factory, Puda Steel Factory, Anli Foreign Company, Wantai Company, Chanshen Foreign Company, Tongji University Factory, Mona Printing Machinery Manufacturing Factory, Li Chang Foreign Company, Gong Chang Iron Factory, China Wireless Research Society, Academia Sinica, Copper and Iron Testing Ground, Weichang Foreign Company, Ford Motor Company, Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant, etc. (2) Railway Exhibition: The displayed trains, rails, and various documents include those from Pinghan, Beining, Daoqing, Pingsui, Longhai, Xiang'e, Nanxun, Jiaoji, Jinghu, Huhangyong, Jinpu, Guangshao, Hangjiang, Zhengtai, Zhushao railways, and the Ministry of Railways. (3) The school's achievements are displayed, including maps of Jiaotong University, new planned buildings, old maps of Nanyang University, and past achievements. (4) Road and Market Exhibition: Includes highway maps of various provinces and cities, public displays of car models, a map of Greater Shanghai, models of the municipal government and various bureaus in the city center. The displays are numerous and cannot be fully listed.

Opening Today: The association will hold the opening ceremony at 10:00 this morning, officiated by Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways. Before the opening ceremony, the opening of the Engineering Hall is scheduled for 9:00 AM, and the completion ceremony of Rong Hong Hall is scheduled for 9:30 AM. The university's regular meeting will be held at 12:30 PM, a national martial arts performance at 2:30 PM, the annual meeting of the Shanghai International Education Association at 4:00 PM, and international songs and educational films from 8:00 PM to 10:00 PM. Those who disrupt the peace and order of the association will not be admitted. 3. A visitor's guide is sold at the entrance of the venue for 30 cents. 4. No advertisements, leaflets, or other promotional materials may be distributed or posted in the venue without the permission of the association. 5. Please do not touch the exhibits without the permission of the exhibitor. 6. Please follow the arrows when visiting. 7. Visitors are requested to observe order. Special attention should be paid to any incidents or crowding. 8. Please do not smoke in or near the shed area. 9. Cars are not allowed to enter the venue. Those who need to enter the venue for official business before the opening or after the closing must first obtain an admission ticket from Mr. Ye Jiajun, the general manager of the association.

General Assembly Declaration: The university is honored by your visit to the Industrial and Railway Exhibition. The initiation of this event was originally intended to commemorate the 35th anniversary of the university's founding. The Shanghai Incident suddenly occurred, and the progress was interrupted. This time, in order to maintain external credibility, the event continues. Preparation was only half done when the incident occurred again. Fortunately, with the special permission of the government, it can be opened on schedule. Efforts for construction should not be changed due to the situation, and the Chinese people should take the opportunity to make a vigorous effort to strengthen themselves after the deep pain of this creation. For plans that can use science to promote development, we must go all out. The university has a related responsibility and dare not abandon its inherent duty. The purpose of this event is to arouse the interest of the Chinese people in engineering and railway undertakings, so as to promote the progress of technology and management methods. At the same time, it can assist the development of industry and commerce, promote the effectiveness of education, connect international feelings, and encourage the spirit of creation. This intention should be understood by everyone. The scale is small, the collection is not complete, but the classification and arrangement are colorful, which is enough to inspire everyone's interest in visiting. We express our warm welcome to all the guests, and with a single thought of the difficult times, we have to encourage everyone to be vigilant in times of adversity. Today, a strong enemy is pressing on the border, and the people's livelihood is poor. The soldiers on the front line are fighting hard in the rain of bullets, and the compatriots in the Northeast are also displaced. We who are fortunate enough to live in peace and work, what should we think about it? We deeply hope that after your visit, you will feel the weight of the national responsibility and make plans for disaster relief and defense according to your financial and intellectual capabilities, so that the foundation of the country can be consolidated and the recovery can be hoped for. This exhibition is limited to engineering and railways. Military supplies that destroy peace have not been included, and decorations that induce luxury have not participated. What is on display is mostly the sharp weapon of production or the necessities of transportation. They are all related to construction issues to some extent. If you observe, compare the advantages and disadvantages, and learn from each other,

Engineering Hall of Jiaotong University (Photo by Xue Huai) 182

Hong Hong Hall of Jiaotong University (Photo by Xue Huai) 183

arouse the idea of ​​improvement and promote the great cause of creation, then this meeting's contribution to China's construction undertakings will be of considerable value. Furthermore, the rapid advancement of modern material civilization is due to the application of science. That is to say, all the exhibits at this meeting are the crystallization of science. Our country's industry is underdeveloped, and production is lagging behind. Looking at this achievement, we should increasingly realize that the study of science cannot be delayed for a day like water and fire. However, water and fire can benefit people today and also hurt people. The effectiveness of science can enrich and strengthen the country, and it can also destroy culture. We should know the power of science and make good use of it. Every instrument and object can create welfare for us and produce more perfect benefits. With the abundance of our country's agricultural products and the richness of our deposits, if we can organize them with scientific methods, the progress will be limitless. This can be inferred from the two aspects of industry and railways. We deeply hope that this exhibition will arouse everyone's interest in research. What is even more advanced is that people from friendly countries have actively participated in this collection, and there are many exhibits that can be used for our reference or exploration. Academics have no borders, which is gratifying. However, we should realize that the mechanical objects needed for engineering and railways can be artificially created, improved, exchanged, and cooperated in. However, if all social problems such as politics, education, law, industry, and commerce cannot be promoted and constructed to achieve the purpose of our ideals, then permanent peace is ultimately unattainable. Therefore, our research on knowledge is not only in natural science and its application, but also should go deep into the halls of social science. This meeting is the third exhibition in the university's brief history. The scale is slightly larger than in the past. The next time it continues to be held, it should be used as a guide. What are your impressions of this meeting? I hope you will make it clear. If you are granted the favor of a compass, you will be especially grateful.

Shanghai School Airplane Realization Is Expected 184

Citywide School Representatives Gathered Yesterday to Discuss

Surplus of Righteous Army Donations Allocated to Purchase Aircraft

Borrowing from the Banking Sector to Purchase First

The Shanghai Municipal Education Association convened a general meeting of representatives from schools throughout the city at the Municipal Education Bureau at 2:00 PM yesterday to proceed with the purchase of the Shanghai School No. 1 military aircraft. More than 300 representatives from over 100 schools, including universities, middle schools, and primary schools, attended. Zheng Hongnian presided, Zhang Lichun acted as the master of ceremonies, and Chen Bangyan kept the minutes.

Report from a Director of the Municipal Education Association 185

After performing the ceremony, Xu Zeyi, a director of the Municipal Education Association, reported on the situation of the righteous army donations, briefly stating that the righteous army donations raised by various schools still amounted to 10,000 yuan. It had previously been proposed to transfer the funds through the Chinese representative office in Moscow, but since there had been no reply from that office, it was impossible to send them. Therefore, the donors were convened to discuss a solution together. Then, Chen Jicheng, a director, reported on the fundraising situation for the Shanghai School aircraft, briefly stating that the Municipal Education Association had previously issued fundraising methods, and since teachers and students from various schools were members of the Aviation Association, it was difficult to raise more funds. Therefore, it was also decided that all funds raised by the Aviation Association in soliciting team leaders from the education sector, as well as funds raised from the education sector by other soliciting team leaders, would be used to purchase the Shanghai School aircraft, so that it could be completed as soon as possible.

Allocation of Righteous Army Donations to Purchase Aircraft 186

The following was immediately resolved: (1) The total amount of Northeast Righteous Army donations handled by the Municipal Education Association was 18,145.8 yuan. After paying 1,060 yuan to the Rehe Anti-Japanese Army and 1,000 yuan to comfort the Anti-Japanese soldiers, the remaining 16,085.2 yuan would be fully allocated to purchase the Shanghai School aircraft.

Borrowing from the Banking Sector to Purchase First 187

(2) The Shanghai School aircraft will be purchased first by borrowing from the banking sector. The Municipal Education Association and Party and government agencies will be responsible for the guarantee, and Liu Zhanen, Zhang Zhongdao, Cheng Kuanzheng, Chen Jicheng, Gu Yinquan, Chen Pinyi, Zhao Luqing, and Wang Dingcheng will be elected to liaise with the banks.
