Shanghai Middle School Association

Record of the Natural Science Discussion Forum 189

The Shanghai Middle School Association in this city holds discussion forums on various subjects each semester to improve the teaching of various subjects. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the schools in the association held a natural science discussion forum at Moore Hall. More than 60 natural science teachers from Shanghai Middle School, Fudan Middle School, Daxia Middle School, Patriotic Girls' School, Chengzhong Middle School, Wuben Girls' Middle School, China Vocational School, Xinmin Middle School, Nanyang Middle School, Guanghua Attached Middle School, Fudan Attached Middle School, Jingye Middle School, Wusong Middle School, Qingxin Middle School, Yucai Middle School, Lida Academy, and Guangzhao Middle School attended. First, Zheng Xigu, a standing committee member of the Middle School Association, reported on the significance of holding the discussion forum and introduced chemical expert Dr. Shao Jialin's lecture on military chemistry, including the history of military poison gas, the types of military poison gas, the inventors and dates of inventions, the analysis of the effects of various poison gases, the limits of poison gas and prevention methods, and how Chinese schools should manufacture poison gas and gas masks. The explanation was very detailed. Then, the meeting elected Shen Yizhen as chairman and Cao Yihua, Yu Junshi, and Shi Bozhu as recorders to discuss natural science issues separately. (1) How to follow the new standards issued by the Ministry. It was resolved to ask Wuben Girls' School to collect the opinions of various schools on the new curriculum standards and then organize them for discussion. (2) How to arouse students' interest to promote science education. The members put forward the following methods: (1) Each school should take turns showing science movies and ask someone to explain them. (2) Each school should encourage students to visit factories, etc. (3) Emphasize experiments. (3) How to introduce the knowledge of modern scientific weapons and gas prevention. It was resolved to (1) visit armories, etc., (2) supplement military physical and chemical teaching materials, (3) study the manufacture of poison gas and gas mask equipment, and recommend Shanghai Middle School to formulate the scope of teaching materials and equipment standards. (4) Natural Science Equipment Standards. It was resolved to recommend Shanghai Middle School to formulate the minimum standards for natural science equipment and submit them to various schools for research and then make a decision. (5) Should a permanent natural science discussion forum or research society be organized to facilitate contact and improve the case? It was resolved to suggest that the Middle School Association organize a natural science research society. The meeting did not end until 5:30 PM.

Sports 196

Sino-British International Shooting Competition

China Scores Successive Victories, Future Optimistic

Zhang Yingda Defeats Nie Ma

Yesterday's Results: 1,000 Points to 737, Victory by 263 Points

Three-Day Summary: China's Score Exceeds by 367 Points

Today, Shen Lince Takes on Maxwell

A Meeting of Famous Experts Is Bound to Have an Amazing Performance

Central China's shooting talents are abundant, and the formal competition with international nature is the first of its kind, sensationalizing men and women from all over the world and creating a grand event in Shanghai's sports world, which is also expected. The three-day competition results show that China has won successive victories, with a total victory of 367 points, and the future is extremely optimistic. Yesterday's scene of Zhang Yingda defeating Nie Ma was particularly brilliant. Today, Shen Lince, a veteran of shooting in our country, is coming out. Mr. Shen was already famous when he studied in England 20 years ago, and he still practices tirelessly, so his experience is particularly rich. Maxwell, the opponent, is one of the famous generals in the UK. In the Group A competition, he always ranks among the best. In a match, regardless of who wins or loses, there will be an amazing performance. The competition will be held twice at 5:30 PM and 9:15 PM in the Shanghai Amateur Shooting Association in the Linhua General Association at No. 3 Beijing Road.

Zhang Yingda is Brilliant

With a Gun in Hand, I Can Do As I Please 197

Zhang Yingda's performance yesterday can be said to be his masterpiece. With a gun in hand, he can do as he pleases. In the first 20 shots, he scored 250 points, averaging 12.5 points per shot. The foundation has been laid, and development is expected. Moreover, no shot is wasted, and the bullet has a path. At 40 shots, he exceeded the opponent by 104 points. At the end of the morning, Mr. Zhang had not finished his shots and was already leading with 500 to 405. After lunch, Mr. Zhang was also oppressed by the opponent for a while, and the distance was reduced to more than 30 points. However, he still used his superb technology in a natural state, and the three huge numbers of 68, 31, and 59 were created from his wrist, creating a large difference in distance of more than 200 points. As a result, he won a total of 263 points.

Nie Ma Suffers a Blow

A Strong Enemy Leads, Defeat Is Still Glorious 198

Nie Ma is defeated, but his skills are good, and heroes cannot be judged by success or failure. The point that he is inferior to Mr. Zhang lies in the time between lightness and weight, thickness and thinness, and right and wrong. The power of the boy's ambition and wrist is still not fully integrated. He is cautious and careful, does not slacken in victory, and is not alarmed in defeat. He has the style of a gentleman. The final failure is also what he deserves, because his skills are still inferior to Mr. Zhang. In the first five shots of the opening, he led the way, and then he fell behind forever and never surpassed. The competition was around 50 or 60 points. Once, when he was more than 100 points behind, he suddenly got 45 points, and the distance was gradually approaching, but he was soon hit again. In the first half, he lost a total of 95 points. At the beginning of the second half, Nie Ma continued to advance, and there was a difference of more than 30 points. Unexpectedly, Mr. Zhang gained the largest amount of 68 points on that day by hitting 43 and 23 points, and from then on, he was in heaven and on earth, and could not be reached. At the end of the war, Nie Ma lost a total of 263 points.

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Talking about National Products

Saving the Nation with Homespun Cloth 210

— Tian Ran

Recently, there have been two very good pieces of news. One is the homespun cloth store initiated by Mr. Zhang Fengshan, the director of the Shanghai Farmers' Education Center, and the other is the homespun cloth improvement association initiated by Mr. Jin Laiwen from Taicang. They both came to me to discuss promotion, and I am very happy. I might as well introduce them: (1) Before there was a homespun cloth store, Mr. Zhang and Mr. Lü Jiren and others first set up a homespun cloth factory in Zhuanqiao called "Green Manure and Red Lean," spinning and weaving themselves. The products are very numerous, very good, and very popular with all parties. However, it is located in a remote rural area, making procurement inconvenient. Mr. Zhang and others then organized a homespun cloth store in Penglai Market. The products in the store all come from the countryside and are woven by the homespun cloth factory itself. The variety of styles is numerous; it can be said that everything is available. At the opening the other day, women in general were very welcoming and adopted it, which is truly very gratifying. (2) After suffering from military disasters, people in Taicang, in order to promote home industry and improve farmers' livelihoods, together with people from Jiading and Baoshan counties, organized a homespun cloth improvement association, lending yarn for weaving. In the past few months, a lot of homespun cloth has been woven. All the products are very sturdy and very cheap, and are unanimously welcomed in various places far and near. They are currently entrusting national products companies and national products introduction centers to promote sales. Looking at it this way, like Gandhi's method in India, promoting it in our country is also very convenient. The saying "saving the nation with homespun cloth" may soon be realized. Mr. Jin has an article called "Saving the Nation with Cloth Clothing," which is earnest and heartfelt and can be used as a reference:

Duke Wen of Wei revitalized the country with coarse cloth clothing, which is a beautiful story in history. Gandhi resisted the British by spinning and weaving homespun cloth, which is an expression of non-cooperation. Ancient and modern, Chinese and foreign, are the same in this regard. The use of coarse cloth is great. Our country is pressured by foreign troubles, and the voice of saving the nation is already clamorous. In particular, resisting enemy goods and promoting national products are the most enthusiastic and widespread. The spirit of perseverance is definitely not comparable to the five-minute enthusiasm of the past. Promoting national products and revitalizing industry are the ways to recover lost interests, while resisting enemy goods and severing economic ties can control the enemy's life. I say that to recover lost interests, there is nothing better than promoting coarse cloth, and to control the enemy's life, there is nothing better than wearing coarse cloth. The raw material for cloth is yarn. Whether the fine yarn raw materials of today's so-called "local factory cloth" are purely national products is a question for research. In our country, apart from the Wing On Spinning Mill and the Shen Xin Spinning Mill, there are very few that can spin fine yarn to supply the raw materials for factory cloth. According to statistics, foreign yarn accounts for 80% of the fine yarn raw materials used by local cloth factories, while local fine yarn, such as Renzhong brand, accounts for only 20%. Examining the reasons, cotton seed improvement has not yet been effective, and the fiber of cotton is short and not strong, making it unsuitable for use in fine yarn, first. Spinning mill technicians can only spin coarse yarn of 20 counts or less. If they spin fine yarn, they must hire people with higher skills, and talent is not easy to obtain, second. Since local cotton is not suitable for use as raw material, and it is not easy to hire technicians, the cost price is therefore high, and the benefit of spinning fine yarn is far less than that of coarse yarn, third. Because of these three reasons, each spinning mill still lacks fine yarn spindle equipment. Even if they have purchased fine yarn spindles, they are all shelved and not used. We are enthusiastically patriotic and promote national products. All uniforms for institutions and schools use local factory cloth instead of foreign wool fabrics. However, 80% of the raw materials for local factory cloth are still inevitably made of foreign fine yarn. The so-called plan to resist enemy goods is still not thorough. For the sake of saving the country at present, to control the enemy's life and sever economic ties, each spinning mill should strive for perfect fine yarn spindle equipment and research the production of fine yarn spinning. At this time when the supply of local factory fine yarn raw materials falls short of demand, all civil servants, school teachers, and students should wear coarse cloth clothing. At celebrations, banquets, commemorative venues, and in front of leading officials and school teachers, they should take the lead in wearing blue cloth gowns and black cloth jackets, then the cloth clothing movement will surely be enthusiastically supported. In the past, Zeng Guofan inspected the Yangtze River wearing a Lingzhuang cloth robe, and Peng Yulin wore a Duoluo hemp arrow jacket during summer military parades. Even now, Lingzhuang cloth and Duoluo hemp are still sold in cloth shops everywhere. Because the leaders took the lead in promoting it, these cloths have been passed down permanently. Moreover, coarse cloth blankets and thorn hairpin cloth skirts, the two words "coarse cloth," are well-known virtues of thrift in our country's history. In the city, high hair buns are popular, with each side a foot high. In the palace, thin waists are popular, and the people reduce their food. Everything depends on the advocacy of those who know and are aware first. Or, it is said that silk raw materials are also natural products of our country. If we promote cloth clothing, the livelihoods of silkworm farmers and weavers will inevitably be affected. It is not known that the cloth clothing movement is originally a temporary plan to save the country, a plan to control the enemy's life, and there is no alternative but to use coarse cloth as a substitute for wool fabrics and factory cloth. At this time when natural disasters occur frequently and chaos is rampant, and the people are not living, it is not harmful to practice thrift. After ten years of recuperation and ten years of teaching, after the marsh of Wu, if material resources are abundant and industry expands, and fine yarn is sufficient to supply the production of cloth factories, then the raw materials used will not be limited to coarse cloth. Those with wealthy family fortunes are not prohibited from wearing local silk and rayon. We can advocate coarse cloth for our own clothing, and we should still advocate improving and expanding the original silk industry as much as possible for foreign trade, to save the precarious state of industry and commerce. Are there those in the world who will approve of my words? I pray for them at the fragrant altar.

Prospects for the National Enamel Industry 211

— Zhou Chengzhu

The enamel industry is in its budding stage. Looking at the fact that we have struggled in a difficult environment to achieve a turnover of six to seven million each year recently, and considering the close relationship between enamel products and daily life, if the situation is peaceful, transportation is convenient, and the purchasing power of the people is widespread, one can imagine how bright and brilliant the future of the enamel industry will be!

To talk about prospects, we must first look back. In Shanghai, many enamel factory chimneys stand tall, working all day long. Past facts tell us that from employing foreign technicians to manufacturing raw materials ourselves, from a few scattered products to an endless stream of styles, this is indeed a page of effort and progress in our country's industrial history. Especially after the Shanghai Incident last year, people in the industry, in view of the scattered pace of their counterparts, reorganized the guild, revised the rules, and improved business and accounting affairs, creating a unique and special organization.

Undoubtedly, competition among counterparts is inevitable in the business world, and the enamel industry is no exception. However, it is already ten thousand times better than other industries. Looking at it from a long-term perspective, this phenomenon of competing for novelty and striving for the lead is ultimately a good indication of striving for progress. It is enough to only hope that it does not fall into the path of infighting and chaotic warfare among counterparts. This is our first point of view for the enamel industry in the National Products Year.

Secondly, if there is a spirit of open cooperation among counterparts, they should earnestly enrich their internal structure. The methods to enrich it are no more than reducing costs and improving work, because we know the importance of enamel products for daily use, and we also know that they have a trend of penetrating into the people. Then, how can the forever high prices and the unmet demand achieve the goal? Examining the current enamel products, they always cannot escape the shortcomings of being crudely made and poorly manufactured. For the sake of passive needs in the market and the pursuit of deer by counterparts, they have to specially make whole batches of sub-standard products to extend the life of the business by cutting flesh to mend sores. Furthermore, because raw materials and labor are expensive, and they cannot think of a way to alleviate the urgent need, the selling price can never be lowered. I think if everyone continues like this, without a concrete strategy to actively save the situation, the result will be terrible. This is our second point of view for the enamel industry in the National Products Year.

There is no shortage of insightful and far-sighted authorities in the enamel industry. Past history is sufficient to prove that the enamel industry is an industry that is more promising than any other, no matter what. If we continue to work hard from our own position, I believe that the National Products Year will be a period of transformation for the enamel industry. I remember what Mr. He Gongxing said in his book (Small Industries in Shanghai): "In the future, when you go deep into the fields, you will see that wine sellers and food deliverers in the village all carry enamel utensils." I also keep this passage in mind and have a deep hope for the enamel industry!

National Products Forum

Thrift Movement and Using National Products 212

— Pan Yang'an

Recognizing that thrift is a virtue, breaking the misconception of only looking at clothes and not people, and many insightful housewives are working hard, this is not only a temporary family reform movement, but also the foundation for building a new and good social custom. Regarding the meaning and value of the thrift movement, we have already clearly acknowledged it, and in the current stage of doing it, of course, we can only do our best!

Speaking of thrift, it involves economics. For objects with the same function, of course, those that are cheap and of good quality are qualified. You can even be more simple and not be extravagant for the sake of winning the fancy. Then, when we choose items, national products and imported goods with the same function (pay attention to foreign goods with ulterior motives), this can give us an applicable standard.

According to general observation, people in cities use several times more imported goods than people in the countryside. In particular, so-called modern young men and women have become promoters of foreign goods. Therefore, residents in the countryside who are warm in cloth clothes and full with vegetable rice do not need to promote thrift and do not indulge their lives. However, the prevailing extravagance in cities and the inferiority of worshiping imported goods are not mutually causal. This is a fact that we should clearly recognize when we are doing the thrift movement.

Using national products is a common virtue among nationals of various countries. Sometimes, they even give up foreign goods that are cheap and of good quality and use their own products, because they have long had a recognition and determination for national products, and naturally can sacrifice themselves for the sake of the entire national economy. Regarding this point, in China, where we are starting to build national confidence in national products, we certainly cannot have extravagant hopes. However, Chinese national products are not more expensive than imported goods, so the thrift movement and using national products can be solved at the same time.

Because worshiping foreign goods and extravagance are mutually causal, and even more because the thrift movement and using national products can be solved at the same time, and there is also a relationship between family economy and national economy, under this cyclical situation, we naturally hope to work hard at the same time, and there is no sacrifice, no contradiction, and it can be mutually reinforcing!

Strive to Eliminate Three Evils 213

— Zhicheng

The emerging Chinese national product production industry is being parasitized by three evils, eroding like tuberculosis germs. We must bring out the spirit of General Zhou!

First: Everywhere is Lu Gaojian. Instead of striving to improve the product, they want to sell money by borrowing other people's signs. As a result, the one being shadowed is the one suffering the loss. Slick goods also fail, harming others without benefiting oneself. We must first eliminate this evil.

Second: Being brave in internal disputes is a characteristic of our noble country, but the production industry cannot be spared. Mr. Zhai Kecong once told a story that electric flashlights were first national products that overcame imported goods, but later they declined because the national product industry reduced materials and prices to compete, and as a result, imported goods still reaped the fisherman's profit. The German production industry has the virtue of not competing internally. It seems that our national product industry should also consider the entire group and eliminate this second major evil.

Third: Changing the appearance is certainly a despicable act. The production industry also likes to use raw materials from imported goods, which is indirectly promoting foreign goods. It is harmful that Dr. Ge Chenghui even feels that removing children is not a genuine national product. This is certainly the action of a few people, but the production industry must have customers firmly believe in national products, and they themselves must be a good example. Moreover, it is related to the reputation of national products, so it is best to (correct them if they exist, and encourage them if they do not) eliminate this third evil!

New Industry Introduction

Introducing a National Factory Manufacturing Elastic Band 214

— Si Sheng

Elastic band, such a small item, when it was completely dependent on Japanese goods four or five years ago, there was an outflow of tens of thousands of yuan every year. Since the emergence of the national elastic band from the Meilun Factory, because of the excellent quality of the products, the Chinese people are happy to use them, and Japanese goods have naturally been gradually eliminated.

The address of the Meilun Textile Factory is in Luqiu Fang, Suzhou. It was founded by Mr. Zhang Zixiang, a Wu native. At first, it specialized in making silk stockings, but it was greatly reduced due to the impact of artificial silk stockings. Later, it changed to making elastic bands, and it happened that the voice of advocating national products in the society was rising day by day, and the business was thriving. Then, it expanded its scope and added capital, and has now become a complete national product factory.

The Meilun Factory currently has about 130 or 40 workers. Its internal organization is led by the Manager's Office and Accounting Room as the highest authorities, managing all the affairs of the factory. Under them are the Engineering Department, Workshop, Ironworking Department, Dyeing Department, Finishing Department, and Engine Room. The Engineering Department specializes in preparing projects, such as shaking weft, warping, twisting rubber bands, winding silk, and twisting silk. All use female workers. The workshop is divided into shuttle weaving and bobbin weaving departments. Shuttle looms have foreign and Chinese types. Weavers are all male workers, and one engineer is hired to be responsible for guidance and supervision. The Ironworking Department is responsible for repairing and manufacturing machines. The Dyeing Department is responsible for dyeing. All use male workers. The Finishing Department does trivial tasks such as sizing, ironing, repairing, and boxing. Use female workers. The Engine Room specializes in generating electricity and is equipped with a motor to make up for the lack of power.

The source of raw materials for elastic bands, except for yarn that can be used from national products, artificial silk and rubber are all imported goods. Its looms, such as jacquard machines, which are more sophisticated, are all ordered from abroad. Its simple and ordinary machines were previously manufactured by Chinese iron factories. The working process, in simple terms, is roughly: first, the Dyeing Department dyes 丨 then it is handed over to the Engineering Department to do various preparatory work, and then it is put on the machine to weave, and finally it is handed over to the Finishing Department for finishing, boxing, and shipping out for sale.

The Meilun Factory employs local runners to sell and promote. A Shen Village is established in Shanghai as a hub for exporting goods and purchasing raw materials. The total business volume reaches more than 200,000 yuan per year. Because the factory is located inland, labor costs are lower than those in Shanghai, and the cost is reduced, so there is quite a surplus. Its sales cover South China, North China, and the Yangtze River Basin, as far as the Nanyang Islands. Since September 18th, sales in North China have suddenly become sluggish due to the impact of the situation and the dumping of Japanese goods. In South China and the Yangtze River Basin, it continues to maintain its advantage in competing with Japanese goods and is not defeated by Japanese goods.

Manufacturing elastic bands is an emerging industry in our country. The Meilun Factory has been established for less than five years and already has such achievements, which is indeed commendable and valuable. Here, on the one hand, we hope that the Meilun Factory will strive for excellence and become more and more developed. At the same time, we also hope that many other national product factories will catch up quickly and strive for the lead. Then, the future of national products will have limitless bright and brilliant hope!

About Domestic Soap 215

— Jie Lu

Soap is a daily necessity. Washing clothes and bathing require soap. The first soaps used in our country were all foreign soaps. Although there were domestic products at that time, they were crudely made and unusable. How could the outflow of benefits every year be less than tens of millions! Later, a German also set up a large soap factory in Xujiahui, Shanghai, preparing for large-scale manufacturing. However, shortly after the opening, the European War suddenly broke out. Because the Germans were going back to their country to participate in the war, Mr. Xiang Songmao, a wealthy Chinese businessman, raised funds to buy the soap factory. This is the current Five Continents Gu Ben Soap Factory.

Because of the completeness of the equipment and the efforts of the person taking over, the Five Continents Gu Ben Soap Factory has been growing day by day under the management of the Chinese people. The power of imported soap has slowly decreased, and domestic Gu Ben soap is already in short supply.

If we carefully study the reasons for the success of Gu Ben soap, it is entirely because the organizer, Mr. Songmao, is willing to take responsibility. For example, regarding the improvement of products, the chemical composition of raw materials, the harmony of oils, and the effectiveness of detergency, there are detailed inspections and research in every aspect. Especially regarding the refining process, the water content of Gu Ben soap is only 25%, while the water content of other inferior soaps is as high as 50%. Therefore, in comparison, Gu Ben soap will never undergo adverse changes.

Undoubtedly, Five Continents Gu Ben Soap can recover benefits and occupy a glorious page in the history of national products.

Visiting Notes

Regarding Rare and Unique National Products 216

— Ke Ding'an

The Republic of China's participation in the Chicago World's Fair product exhibition had already started last month on Bailinan Road. However, due to the current critical national crisis, the exhibition was unfortunately ordered to cease, which is truly disappointing!

The China National Products Company was established during this eventful year for national products. It was understood that it would not have great power to accomplish earth-shattering events and compete with the Shanghai market, which is saturated with foreign goods. However, its mission is quite commendable: to promote the glory of China's national products and develop outlets for them. It also aims to collect local specialties from various regions as much as possible, striving to become the most comprehensive national products company in the country.

The exhibitors who were to participate in the Chicago World's Fair were understandably very disappointed by this setback. However, in line with its mission, the China National Products Company collaborated with the exhibitors to hold a re-exhibition on the second floor of its southern section. The exhibition period ended yesterday, and the exhibitors have made considerable arrangements to go to the United States independently. It would be truly gratifying if Chinese products receive awards and return with honor from Chicago!

Although the product exhibition at the China National Products Company lasted only a brief fourteen days, it was indeed memorable. Friendly nations' representatives accounted for as much as 40% of the daily visitors, which shows that Chinese products have many aspects that can be appreciated by international friends. We Chinese people should be ashamed if we do not support national products!

The exhibited products were numerous. Just taking the words of Guan Hong, a representative from Jiangxi, who said, "There are more than 250 boxes of porcelain," as proof, one can get a general idea.

Now, I will introduce what I consider to be rare and unique national products, listed in order. This is merely a "drop in the ocean" or, perhaps, "missing much while covering a little"!

The grass-woven handbags, purses, and baskets produced by Zhenxing Xian Ji in Xuhang Town, Jiading, are exquisitely woven with appropriate patterns! The tables and chairs produced by the Senlin Rattan Willow Grass Utensil Factory are made of willow, painted in light beige, and have coffee-colored tabletops and matching lines. In terms of color, they are beautiful and elegant; in terms of style, they are unique and refined, worthy of being called masterpieces of the new era. Hunan paper umbrellas have long been famous. However, the umbrellas with vermilion-lacquered bodies, brass-wrapped tops, and rattan handles are no longer suitable for modern use. They have skillfully adapted to the trend and produced many novel paper umbrellas. The ones for women are especially beautiful, with particularly bright colors and patterns. Even the long tassels on the umbrella handles are matched with the colors of the umbrella handle and body. The ones for children are small, exquisite, light, and interesting. Many children pull on their accompanying parents to buy them, but because these paper umbrellas are not for sale, the children are helpless!

"Chinese tea" has always been highly valued in the eyes of foreigners. However, due to unscrupulous merchants who prioritize profit over the future by mixing impurities into the exported tea, foreigners have seen through this, causing the reputation of Chinese tea to plummet and giving other countries an excellent opportunity to promote their tea.

The famous tea merchant Wang Yu Chang also had products on display, including several precious varieties such as "Lianfeng Sangrui," "Weiyan Kuding," "Mantou Pu'er," "Wenzhou Baihao," "Longtuan Pu'er," "Biluochun," and others.

The products from the Jiangxi Fuxing Company were perhaps the most numerous. The carvings on the camphor wood chests are exceptionally detailed. Motifs such as "Lotus," "Pine and Crane," "Five Steeds," "Two Qiaos," and "Imitation Han Bricks" are beyond the skills of ordinary craftsmen. Summer cloth, gauze, and other items are also excellent. Regarding porcelain, there are ancient pieces such as "Song Ding Kiln Bowls," which are light blue with faint patterns; "Tang Yingqing Bowls," which appear white at first glance but are faintly blue upon closer inspection; and "Southern Tang Yonghe Porcelain Bowls," of which there are two types: one with an uneven rim resembling an opening lotus flower, with a dark brown color and faint black patterns, and the other black with unclear white patterns. The "Tang Yingqing Huxiao Bottle" is about 1.5 feet tall with a mouth diameter of about three inches. It is light blue with excellent luster, patterns on the waist, and pointed angular patterns on the neck, which are very meaningful. The price is 100,000 yuan. The "Qinghua Bowl Made in the Jiajing Year of the Great Ming Dynasty" is dark brown with fine crackles. The "Caihua Bowl Made in the Da Ming Year of the Northern Qi Dynasty" has a white body, ochre red double lines on the bottom and rim, and a plum blossom with a crescent moon in the center of the bottom circle, which is quite interesting.

There were many Guanyin statues on display. My favorite is the one from "Purple Bamboo Grove," with a base diameter of about eight inches. The surface is meticulously carved with a purple bamboo grove in the back and a lotus pond in the front. Guanyin stands in front of the purple bamboo grove, holding a willow branch, with a graceful and ethereal expression full of celestial charm. A child stands on the opposite bank, making a bow with both hands. The carving has truly reached a realm of perfection.

Also remarkable is the "Song Longquan Empty Bottom Bowl," with a diameter of about seven inches, standing upright on a mahogany stand. The color is light green, and the bottom is empty. If it is placed upside down on a table, it looks like a modern water container. The bottom edge is dark brown, and the bowl is priced at 1,400 yuan.

The depictions of birds and animals are very lifelike. The most striking are the white geese, with their large buttocks almost touching the ground and their necks stretched out, calling. Their feathers are made as realistically as real ones. The prices are "three yuan" and "ten yuan." One of them is relatively small; judging by the exhibitor's affectionate expression, it is probably not for sale!

There are also many large porcelain vats. One is the "Imperial Kiln Golden Red Dragon Thousand-Piece Vat," priced at 1,000 yuan, which is very lovely. There is also a Bian Yao bottle, of which the exhibitor said, "It is difficult to find one like this even if thousands of bottles are fired." This is indeed true. The bottle is about nine inches tall and over a foot in circumference. The bottom of the bottle is white, the neck is brown, and the body is tinged with "brown" and "red," with distinct layers of cloud patterns, which are simply rare masterpieces.

There are also thousands of other items such as paintings, porcelain panels, portraits, hanging screens, tea sets, fruit, stationery, and large vases, which are truly dazzling. The products of He Wengun excel in their exquisite smallness. The "White Carved Porcelain Flower Basket" has a base diameter of about five inches, filled with many flowers, each facing upwards. The peony best displays its former majestic kingly demeanor. There is also the "Kangxi Jicui Temple Top," which is circular, about seven inches high, and about one foot and two inches in circumference, with a very bright sky-blue color.

The lacquerware produced by Wu Rongsheng in Yangzhou is extraordinary. The most precious is the "Inlaid Eight Treasures Zhou Pillar Figure Screen," made in the early Daoguang period, which has a very ancient feel. The carving and inlaying are truly remarkable. The exhibitor marked it with the four words "Rare Treasure," which are very suitable for the work. There are many types of stationery, small round tables, fan-shaped stools, and complete sets of square plates, all inlaid with mother-of-pearl patterns and carvings, which are worth playing with.

Fujian's lacquerware has a long-standing reputation. The products of the Huier Orphanage received many positive reviews this time. The statues include "Confucius," "Laozi," "Mozi," "Three Stars," "Sun Yat-sen," "Guan Yu" – both sitting and standing statues, and I think the standing ones are more spirited. "Longevity Star," "Damo," "Tieguai," "Luozu," "Qi Jiguang" – seeing General Qi's majestic appearance makes me think of the present situation and I can't help but shed tears! "Amitabha," and others each have their own unique postures, which can express the spirit of each figure. Here, one can see the author's meticulousness. There are also several masterpieces: "Cowherd and Cow," with every detail of the cow's hair meticulously rendered. The cowherd's lively state is different in each piece, which is also rare.

Yixing pottery, in the hands of Chen Hongshou Mansheng during the Qing Dynasty, had many masterpieces that he shaped with his own hands, but their current prices are very expensive! This time, the Yixing Vocational School Pottery Department has many new products, such as "teapots, teacups, tea trays," "vases," "flower inserts," "assembled bowls," each with dozens of varieties, and the patterns painted on them are the latest designs. There is also a "Sun Yat-sen Statue," which is made vividly and realistically.

Zhou Shaofu's small decorations in Wuxian can well express China's unique style. This time, he participated with a Yuan Yang Hall, which included specially made tables, shelves, chairs, stools, tea sets, cabinets, and furnishings, as well as calligraphy, paintings, screens, couplets, qin, chess, silk bamboo instruments, etc., which probably cost more than several thousand gold.

The display method of the antique section is unique, and the display stands are specially made of rosewood. Among them, what makes people reluctant to leave are the "Large and Small Crystal Balls on Rosewood Stands," and the "Jade Carved Great Mountain," with mountains, trees, figures, and landscapes as vivid as a painting, with deep green colors, which are truly divine. The "Guanyin Statue" is also carved from jade, with ancient-style clothing and appearance. It would be even more valuable if the color were greener. There is also the "Zhou Dynasty Jue Ding," a "Copper Washing Basin of the Han Dynasty," and an "Ancient Copper Panlong Vase," with a dragon raising its head, wanting to enter the clouds, which is very powerful. The "Carved Sailing Boat" is made by carving a section of Mao bamboo. An Old Man of the South Pole sits in the boat, holding a peach in his right hand, with a pleasant smile. A servant boy sits on the stern, very leisurely. The boat is about eight inches long, and the carving is excellent.

There are also silk fabrics from the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, cotton fabrics from Sanyou, Samsung, Hongxin, China Underwear Company, and Chinese specimens, which are all breathtaking.

Finally, I must state that because I looked at them in a hurry, I could not introduce them to the fullest extent. I have already said that it is merely "a drop in the ocean" and "missing much while covering a little," so I will not dwell on it further.

Editor's Note

The Tang Monk's Journey to the West My old friend Chi Zongmo once said that running a national products business is as difficult and dangerous as the Tang Monk's journey to the West to seek scriptures. When sea transport was not available, communication between China and India was cut off, the Kunlun and Himalayas were two barriers, extremely high, and the shifting sands were thousands of miles, with ice covering the mountains, the Tang Monk had great faith and made great vows, one robe, one bowl, running thousands of miles, and finally reached the Buddhist kingdom. He also relied on the three-headed and six-armed Sun Wukong, the large-eared and long-mouthed Pig Bajie, and the strong Sha Wujing as his disciples, supporting him from the front and back, and supporting him from the left and right, before he succeeded. Therefore, those who run factories should learn from the Tang Monk's perseverance and seek versatile and loyal Sun Wukong, Pig Bajie, and Sha Wujing as their assistants. Mr. Chi's words are worth encouraging those who run national products businesses.

Women Rise Up Women have the most profound relationship with national products, and the right to use them is in their hands. Last time I heard Dr. Ge Chenghui's lecture, she said: "If a husband insists on buying foreign goods, the wife can file for divorce to deal with him." These words are really refreshing and can serve as a wake-up call for men who love to use foreign goods. We have decided to publish a special issue on "Women and National Products" to show our promotion, hoping that our female compatriots will rise up and do something.

Spring and Autumn

A Decaying Household 217

— Hua Ling

"A family that passes down poetry and rites," "A scholarly family" – these signs, these hard signboards, in this day and age, have no other use than to be thrown into the latrine. A decaying household is shameful. A nouveau riche is popular.

Indeed, the sixth and seventh ancestors, reaching a position below one person and above ten thousand, were truly incomparably prestigious. But if the descendants are not ambitious, generation after generation, pawning and selling, eating and using, becoming accustomed to vulgarity, not seeking advancement, ending up neither cultured nor martial, neither high nor low, the broken doorway is filled with hard signs such as "A family that passes down poetry and rites" and "A scholarly family." What use are they? If the neighbor of this decaying household suddenly prospers and becomes a nouveau riche, then, whether they came from driving a cart or running a brothel, local celebrities and gentry will rush to become sworn brothers, connect genealogies, and enthusiastically flatter them. When the nouveau riche builds a house, encroaching on the land of the decaying household, and the decaying household refuses, the nouveau riche will break their head. Even though the gentry has been friends with the decaying household for generations, they will help the nouveau riche and advise the decaying household to compromise.

Our China has a history of thousands of years of culture, worthy of being "A family that passes down poetry and rites" and deserving of "A scholarly family." But other than that, having exhausted everything, possessing nothing, it presents a living picture of a decaying household. And Japan, with its diligent men and frugal women, has become an upstart that cannot be ignored. They become sworn brothers with the gentry-like England, America, France, and Germany, connect genealogies, and treat each other as equals. In the September 18th Incident, the January 28th Incident, and all the acts of invasion and plunder, how is it that the decaying household is not beaten bloody by the nouveau riche every time? How is it that the gentry who call the nouveau riche brothers do not advise the decaying household-like China to compromise every time? The nouveau riche encroaches on land, injures people, and remains unpunished. The decaying household suffers losses and endures humiliation. What can they do besides swallowing their voices, shedding tears, and suppressing their anger? The unambitious decaying household, at the slightest provocation, brandishes hard signs such as "A family that passes down poetry and rites" and "A scholarly family," truly disgracing the sixth and seventh ancestors!

Acute and Chronic Poisoning 218

— Bing Ding

If we eat arsenic or mercury, we will immediately bleed from all seven orifices, have abdominal pain and dizziness, and die. This is called "acute poisoning." Greedy friends who eat pufferfish or poisonous mushrooms still think they taste very delicious, indescribable, not knowing that the poison will soon take effect. The wronged ghosts of the pufferfish and poisonous mushrooms will come to claim your life as quickly as Yan Xijiao captures Zhang Sanlang. This is also called "acute poisoning." Friends who have tuberculosis or old smokers who inject morphine and smoke red pills, although the King of Hell does not come to invite you to have fun for a while, you have already been marked. In the near future, you will be a guest of honor in the Yama's palace! This is called "chronic poisoning."

It is reported that someone picked up an English letter from Jia Chuangsai Qi to Xian Erlaisen at the Zuiontei Hotel in Yokohama, Japan. It roughly said: "In October 1931, a Poisoning China Radical Drug Research Society was established in a certain Japanese medical school. Its purpose is to use scientific methods to put all kinds of poisons into human necessities. Among them, the toxins can cause lifelong infertility; i.e., the poison is hidden in clothing materials. There are also those that can cause cholera; such as cosmetics or utensils, which contain this kind of bacteria. Harming the Chinese people is insidious, and it can be seen generally; we who live in China should also be more careful!" It also said: I have telegraphed the government to arouse people's attention to this kind of talk. Originally, the Japanese are the most cunning and insidious, and it is inevitable that they will not follow the old trick of Wang Fengzhou poisoning Yan Donglou. Is the discovery of this letter not giving us a "warning"?

We must know that we like to use enemy goods for the sake of cheapness, which is "chronic poisoning," that is, "chronic suicide," and what is the difference between injecting morphine, smoking red pills, and developing tuberculosis! Now, the Japanese are impatient, thinking that it is too annoying for the Chinese to slowly become extinct and perish, so they simply put some poisons into the goods that the Chinese love to use, so as not to suffer from "chronic poisoning" of "sleeping pigs," (the Japanese call me that honor) suffer every day, groan every day, and go to the Western Paradise early (maybe it is Jewish). This is the Japanese's good intention, and we must not misunderstand it!

Talking About Invisibility 219

— Zheng Yimei

Yesterday at a banquet, I heard Fang Benchu, a student who studied in Germany, say: "A philosopher in Berlin recently invented a kind of invisibility, which is really a strange story from abroad. This philosopher made a special suit and a special mask. When he puts them on and goes to a friend's house, the friends hear the sound but cannot see him." But I don't know what material this suit and mask are made of? It actually has such a mysterious effect. Science is really omnipotent! It is a pity that there is still a kind of sound. If there is no such sound, wouldn't it be better!

Invisibility is an old saying that has always existed in our country. Lang Huan Ji: "After Lord Father wore barbarian clothes, he often observed the celestial phenomena at night. One night, a divine man descended from the sky and授Lord Father with the art of invisibility." But it has never been discovered in fact. If there is really such a kind of invisibility, then this invisible person will be able to do whatever he wants alone. Rich families, precious treasures and ornaments can be arbitrarily obtained, and beautiful concubines and charming Ji can be entertained. Wouldn't the rich and powerful be terrified?

I remember a joke from the past: "A person learned the art of invisibility from a magician and returned home. After performing the magic, he asked his wife, 'Can you see me?' His wife said, 'You are standing in front of me, how can I not see you?' The person thought that the magic was not correct, and 重行 drew symbols and burned incantations. When he asked his wife again, his wife answered as before. After doing this several times, his wife was quite annoyed and said that she could not see him. The person was very proud and ran out. Seeing the meat hanging in the butcher shop, he tried to take a pig's trotter, but he didn't get the meat and was beaten by the butcher."

Japan is a country with a conscription system. In recent years, it has been engaged in militarism and implemented a nationwide general mobilization. Therefore, the recruitment of new soldiers is very popular, but the Japanese have come up with various methods to avoid joining the army, either turning their eyes into deep myopia or starving themselves to reduce their body weight, because those with myopia and weak bodies are not qualified to join the army. There is also a kind of superstition. If you want to avoid joining the army, ask a thirty-three-year-old woman to pluck three hairs and wrap them in red cloth, sew them into the placket of the clothes, which is a kind of invisibility that can avoid the inspector's poisonous eyes, which is so ridiculous!

The Logic of Life 221

— Xu Benxi

We can see very beautiful people arguing with rickshaw drivers or vendors over one or two pennies. Or, if you're unlucky, they might even raise their hands and slap them once or twice. From a positive perspective, it seems that Shanghainese are so thrifty that they even consider one or two pennies.

In fact, let's put aside the bourgeoisie. Have you ever seen a young man in a suit bending down to pick up a penny that fell in public? On the other hand, in the barber shop, the price is four jiao, but you want to give them one yuan, and when you eat in a restaurant, the tip is already included in the bill, but you still give the waiter the change. Is this extra gift a traditional rule? Or is it a habit that must be possessed by the beautiful class living in the city? Philosophers and philosophers, it really makes me puzzled.

Similarly, satisfying life, decoration and eating are more superior to walking more. How advanced is this metaphysics? In fact, to put it bluntly, a person who is happy to bargain with a rickshaw driver for one or two pennies will definitely not pretend to be bourgeois and show off. How many people in Shanghai care about every penny when dealing with the working class but spare no expense when decorating themselves? The logic of life in Shanghai adds another contradictory example.

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 222

In the third chapter, he finally bears the heart to solve the problem and enters the door. He wrongly secretly pities the maid and is willing to share food as a reward.

This is definitely not a false statement. Denying it cannot be denied, but admitting it is not convenient to admit, so he had to say with a stern face: This is the rogue in my family, how can he say such a thing. I will definitely punish him heavily when I go back. Guizhi looked at her mother, but said: How can you blame the people below, the people above have no words, how dare the people below say such a thing? Ji Zhi said: I just came back from the government, I don't know these things at all, I will ask clearly when I go back, and then come and apologize to the old girl. Guizhi said: We are satisfied with these few words from the second master, please don't ask when you go back, if you ask something bad, you will add something wrong to us. Our mother and daughter are poor and people in the bedroom, and there is nowhere to go if we make trouble. Speaking, his voice hardened, and he pulled out a handkerchief from under his ribs and rubbed his eyes again. At this time, even though Ji Zhi wanted to use words to comfort people, he felt that he had no way to speak, and stood blankly in the house, unable to say a word. In the past, Jiang Shi always treated Ji Zhi with extra courtesy, but today his attitude was very cold. Ji Zhi stood in the middle of the house, standing with nothing to do, and could not use any language to comfort them. At this time, their mother and daughter, one lowered her head and sat weeping, and the other lowered her head to mend clothes. Ji Zhi was always standing here, and he also felt bored, so he bowed his hands to Jiang Shi and said: Thousands of apologies, ten thousand apologies, I am always sorry, please forgive the old girl, I really don't know about this. If I am at home, this kind of thing will never happen. Speaking, he walked out listlessly. (27)

World Rare News

— Chu Yu

Kingdom of Bicycles 223

We all probably know that the global kingdom of automobiles is the United States. This is because the United States has so many cars, with an average of one car for every six people. When it comes to bicycles, the Netherlands must be mentioned first. According to a recent survey, the total number of bicycles in the Netherlands is 2,858,569, while the population of the Netherlands is only eight million, averaging 35 bicycles per 100 people, which means there is one bicycle for every three people.

The Pope's Dairy Cow 224

Pope Pius XI of Rome recently purchased 24 dairy cows, one of which is pure white, spotless and flawless. The Pope designated this cow for his sole use and took great care of it. In the summer, the cow is kept at the Ganderhof farm in the summer resort, and it is led from the farm to the Vatican Palace twice a day to provide milk.

Italian Prime Minister's Library 225

The library of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini contains more than 3,000 books on Fascism. On the tenth anniversary of the March on Rome, the Fascist Academy of Arts and Sciences organized a dedicated Fascist library, now known as the Mussolini Library.

Kissing to Console the Sick 226

An Austrian man named Johannes fell ill and was admitted to the Vienna Hospital for treatment. After more than two months, his condition did not improve. His wife's friend, a beautiful widow, heard that Johannes had been ill for a long time and went to visit him at the hospital. However, she had no other relationship with Johannes. However, when she visited him, she always kissed Johannes twice, once when she arrived and once when she left, as a gift for visiting him. Later, Johannes' wife found out and became very jealous, so she filed for divorce in court. The judge ruled that "kissing the sick is acceptable" and dismissed the lawsuit. From then on, kissing another person's wife in the Vienna Hospital was not only not considered taboo, but also considered very fashionable.

Losses from Fog 227

London is the most famous place in the world for fog. According to a survey by the London Chamber of Commerce, the daily loss caused by fog in London is as high as five million yuan. This is due to the "fog, which hinders commercial traffic, doubles the consumption of electric lights, and causes indirect major losses such as citizens often getting sick.

The Popularity of Artificial Nails 228

Paris, France, is the most prosperous metropolis in the world and the birthplace of the latest trends. Recently, a new fashion item has emerged, and all fashionable women are wearing gold, silver, or other brightly colored artificial nails on their fingers. Currently, stores in Paris that manufacture artificial nails are doing exceptionally well, and everyone is racking their brains to come up with various styles to cater to the psychology of fashionable women. This strange phenomenon will probably spread to Shanghai soon.

Postcard Park 229

The postcard was invented by Hermann, a famous scholar from Austria. Mr. Hermann died thirty years ago, so the world has gradually forgotten his contributions. Recently, a park was built in Vienna called the Hermann Memorial Park. At the entrance of the park, many postcards are collected to build a monument. On the surface of the monument, the words "Hermann, the inventor of the postcard, born in 1839, died in 1902" are engraved.

Injections to Satisfy Hunger 230

The Soviet Union has come up with a way to reduce food consumption due to food shortages. A scholar named Qiukexifu invented a method of satisfying hunger with injections. After receiving the hunger-satisfying injection, one can go without food for two or three days without feeling hungry.

Powdered Wheat Market Continuously Declining with a Slight Rebound 246

The Rebound of Imported Wheat Is Not Without Its Significance

After the afternoon opening of the flour market, prices for various months showed signs of stabilization. Due to the price of imported wheat rising by two, three, or four jiao, the sentiment in the near term immediately appeared brisk after the opening. As actual sales remain active, there may not be an excess of goods for this month, which stabilizes sentiment and improves buying interest. For distant months, manufacturers limited their sales, and speculators covered their positions, tightening the market. Near-term prices rose by seven and a half li, and distant prices rose by about one fen. However, by the afternoon opening, the market for various months showed signs of weakness. Because delivery is approaching for this month, some non-industry speculators are exiting the market, causing prices to level out. As for distant months, there is concern about the dumping of imported wheat, and non-industry buying interest has waned. The overall outcome depends on the source of imported wheat. As a result, this month's price is up five li from the previous day, April's up one fen, May's up seven and a half li, June's up one fen and two and a half li, and July's up five li.

After the morning and afternoon openings of the wheat market, prices for various months showed signs of being close to level and stable. With the price of imported wheat rebounding by two, three, or four jiao, sentiment turned stable. Due to the surge of imported wheat in April, the market showed signs of oversupply, so the market was flat and buying interest was weak. For distant months, the price increase of imported wheat led some short sellers to cover their positions slightly, which tightened the market. However, this localized rise and fall cannot be considered conclusive. As a result, this month's price is down one fen from the previous day, May and June were not opened, July's up one fen, and August's up two fen.

Page 17

Free Talk

On Forgetfulness 257

— Yu Dafu

The "five-minute enthusiasm" refers to the Chinese people forgetting any extreme humiliation after five minutes. Like the woodcutter of Mount Nanke, although the length of time is somewhat different, both are examples of forgetfulness. Speaking of forgetfulness, it does not seem to be a unique characteristic of the Chinese people. I remember seeing an anecdote in the stories of German writers:

The playwright and literary critic Lessing was once taking a walk after writing. On the way, he met a postman delivering letters. "Do you have a letter for me?" Lessing asked. "What is your name, sir?" the postman asked in return. Lessing scratched his head and thought for a long time, but he could not remember his own name. So he had to say with a wry smile, "Let me go home and ask."

This kind of absent-mindedness after focusing one's attention seems to be common to people of all countries, but Chinese forgetfulness is more practical. For example, when warlord infighting begins, both sides issue telegrams, each cursing the other with the most venomous language, vowing to never coexist. But soon after, they turn hostility into friendship, and in an instant, they call each other brothers, with affection surpassing flesh and blood. The warlords are like this, and so are the politicians. We only need to pull out old newspapers and flip through them to see many such facts. When the National Revolutionary Army arrived in Shanghai, the propaganda posters were full of depictions of the Northern Warlords that they sought to overthrow. They drew a turtle with the name of a warlord on its shell. After the change of flags, however, Zhang San and Li Si were all comrades. Zhang Zongchang, who had an arrest warrant issued against him, was given a pension by the government after he was killed. Someone avenging his father was granted a special pardon by the state. After the May Fourth Movement, everyone advocated filial impiety, but now the articles of the Constitution stipulate that sons have the duty to respect their parents. Apart from this pragmatic forgetfulness, general forgetfulness is indeed beneficial to us humans in many ways.

First, the most common fact is that if something terrible happens at night, after one night, when you get up in the morning and see the sun, everything is dispelled, and the matter that was so urgent seems to have a way out. This is an experience that everyone often encounters. Second, the pain of life and death is known to all. Fortunately, healthy people forget death, so they go to run businesses and form societies. Women forget the pain of childbirth, so they go on to have second and third children, preserving the race. The modern British essayist Robert Lynd also talked about these things in an essay entitled "The Pleasures of Ignorance." Here, I would like to change the last word to Forgetfulness, calling it "The Pleasures of Forgetfulness." The most concrete proof of this topic is the Summer Palace, which the Empress Dowager Cixi built after the defeat, using funds from the navy. Now the Japanese imperialist army seems to only use the Great Wall as a boundary, and will no longer invade the south. I do not know, for the sake of saving the country through aviation, whether the many patriotic donations obtained by the movie queen and others advocating entertainment to save the country will be used to build a second Summer Palace in Lushan or West Lake.

Street Exhibitions 258

— Shi Heng

On the streets, on the streets of this most prosperous city in the East, have you often seen those ugly exhibitions that make people unable to bear to look at, those various disabled people?

On the wide roads, trams and cars are speeding, and on the sidewalks on both sides, there are crowds of people coming and going. Among the clothes of these pedestrians, there are always disabled people sitting or crawling. They have either lost an arm, broken a leg, gone blind, or have festering flesh. Their heads are almost always bowed to the ground, facing the passing pedestrians, hoping that someone might take out one or two copper coins from their pockets and drop them into the alms bowl placed in front of them. But it is not easy to get someone to drop money in, so they cry bitterly, moan, and especially show the ugliest and most pitiful parts of their bodies in order to gain human sympathy. If these existing disabilities are not enough to arouse people's pity, then they will pretend to accidentally, but in fact deliberately, re-injure some part of their body, and fresh blood drips on the ground. When their nerves feel a kind of unbearable pain, their roar and their lament can also make pedestrians feel real and tragic. Then, his alms bowl will be able to receive a few more copper coins! I have personally seen a disabled person with half a leg crawling in front of the gate of a school, deliberately breaking his nose on the stone steps. Blood splashed on the ground, and he lay there motionless, as if facing the sky, and as if facing cruel humanity, crying, scolding, and weeping. That hoarse voice and that tragic scene made those who saw and heard it feel as if they were in a ferocious hell.

I never bear to hear such lamentations or tragic situations, and I never bear to look at them. To me, they are like demons, making me avoid them, so, I honestly say, I have never given a penny to such disabled people. Because I absolutely do not have the courage to approach them, even if I close my eyes and drop money into their alms bowl. Sometimes, I catch a glimpse from afar or just realize that there is such an ugly shape lying ahead, and my nerves will immediately convulse, casting a heavy shadow on my heart.

I remember when I was reading literary history before, the Romantics or Idealists taught us that the task of writers should be to try to hide or avoid observing the ugliness of reality, and to create works that beautify life. Perhaps this is reasonable, but not in our current society. Can you stay in a house for the rest of your life and not go out to the streets once? And how can you avoid seeing this ugly exhibition on the streets? What ugliness of reality is greater than this?

It is impossible to hide, and there is no need to hide, all the sores of this existing society. Someday, the roars of these ugly disabled people will drag down this entire cruel society.

An Explanation of "Attempt" 259

— Cao Juren

Lu Fangweng's poem says, "Attempting success has never happened since ancient times." Hu Shi gave it a turn of phrase: "Success has always been in attempting." He also said: "I have sought teachers for twenty years, and now I have obtained the two words 'attempt': one must do poetry and business like this, and although one may not reach it, one still has ambition." Lu Fangweng's personal experience was very deep. Seeing the country broken and the family destroyed, and the situation getting worse day by day, those who sold the country for peace were truly "without hearts or livers," and those who were patriotic and advocated war were just "shouting empty slogans that did not hit the mark." So he said indignantly, "Attempting success has never happened since ancient times!" What he meant was that saving the country required a whole plan, to be done practically and realistically. Relying on luck and taking shortcuts would not succeed. (The meaning is very clear, please see the original poem.)

And our Dr. Hu Shi learned the secret of living from the opposite side of this poem. He saw that Chinese society was a chaotic society, and nothing was on track. To appear on stage and become a big figure in this society, the first thing to do is to speculate. For example, buying a lottery ticket, winning the jackpot, wouldn't you be very rich? If you never buy a lottery ticket in your life, you will never have the hope of winning the jackpot. The jackpot comes from buying a lottery ticket. This is what Dr. Hu Shi called: "Success has always been in attempting." Which is what Shanghai people call "trying your luck."

Our Dr. Hu Shi, he has won the jackpot. There are many students studying in the United States, but he alone has become a new cultural guide, a member of the Sino-British Cultural Fund Committee, and a member of the Peking Political Branch. There are many other benefits. When he took a trip to Hunan, he received a special offering of five thousand yuan. This is what he himself said: "I have sought teachers for twenty years, and now I have obtained the two words 'attempt': one must do poetry and 'business' like this, and although one may not reach it, one still has ambition." We congratulate him: "Ambition eventually succeeds!"

Since the May Fourth Movement, people have all "attempted" and "speculated" everywhere. This is the best achievement of the New Culture Movement! Alas!

(Note) There is a great deal of evidence that Hu Shi spent his life watching the wind and hanging the sail, speaking according to the opportunity. Please refer to my recently compiled Hu Shi Literary Genealogy.

Tengwang Pavilion 260

— Ms. Wen Juan

As soon as I arrived in Nanchang, I went to look for Tengwang Pavilion, but after walking all over Nanchang City, I still didn't know where the world-famous Tengwang Pavilion was. So I silently recited the words of Wang Bo's preface and searched along the riverbank. When I reached the front of the Water Public Security Bureau, I met an old man and went up to ask:

"Old man, do you know where Tengwang Pavilion is?" The old man sighed.

"This is Tengwang Pavilion! You don't know even when you see it!" He pointed to the small and humble Public Security Bureau building and said with emotion.

However, I was still confused. It was clearly the Public Security Bureau, so how could he insist that it was Tengwang Pavilion? After the old man's explanation, I realized that this building of historical value had long been destroyed by war. Later, someone built this Water Public Security Bureau on the original site of the pavilion.

The old man continued:

"This pavilion was built in the fourth year of the Xianqing era of the Tang Dynasty, when Prince Teng Yuan Ying was the governor of Hongzhou (Nanchang's ancient name was Hongzhou). It originally had two pavilions, an outer pavilion on Chao Wang Zhou (which collapsed in the Tang Dynasty) and an inner pavilion, which was this Tengwang Pavilion. In the second year of the Xianting era of Emperor Gaozong of Tang, Yan Boyu, the governor of Hongzhou, renovated the pavilion once, and Wang Bo's preface was written at that time. Later, Emperor Taizu of Ming visited Nanchang once after 'universal peace,' and held a grand banquet for his meritorious officials in this pavilion, and released a deer raised by Chen Youliang to Xishan. His ministers catered to his psychology and built a large archway in front of the pavilion, titled 'The First Building Under Heaven.' It suffered a fire during the Wanli era, which almost destroyed most of it. It was rebuilt in the early Qing Dynasty, until the most recent fire six years ago, which finally ended its life." The old man coughed and continued:

"In the past, transportation was inconvenient, and when there were no trains, most people who went out traveled by water. This pavilion was next to the river, and the terrain was good. Whenever someone was seeing off a guest, they would set up a banquet in front of this pavilion for the farewell. It has been like this throughout the ages. Now, alas! Alas! Everything is over." The old man shook his head as he said this, and then continued to mutter something, before slowly walking eastward.

I stood blankly in front of this abandoned pavilion, thinking about the old man's last words, and couldn't help but have many fantasies: this small pavilion, I don't know how many words of reluctant farewells it has heard, how many parting tears it has seen. If the pavilion had consciousness, it would probably be overwhelmed by them! Oppressed by these sorrows of separation until it could not breathe! Even if it did not suffer from war, it would probably be crushed by sorrow. Now that it has been burned down, it is clean. Who can say that a soldier is necessarily a person who spoils the scenery!

Only those two rivers of different colors and different temperaments (the confluence of the Fu and Gan rivers, one yellow and one clear, never mixing), still rely on each other day and night, probably having seen enough of the pain of separation at the top of the building, and will never dare to separate!

The Age of Long Novels and the Crossroads of Love 261

— Zhang Ziping

The car turned a few corners on the small streets, drove onto the road, increased its speed, and turned again after a while. Haiquan was sitting in the car and couldn't see clearly which road it was. He just intuitively felt that the car had circled a few times in the area around Daxi Road and Hege Road, and then stopped in front of a Western-style house. Everyone got out of the car. Yaoxing sent the car away and then pressed the doorbell for a while. At this time, Haiquan saw that not far from the front of this house, there was a patrolman standing there, not paying much attention to someone coming here in a car.

After waiting for a while, a Western woman opened the door and came out to greet them.

"What is this place?"

He asked Yaoxing.

"Don't be nosy. Just follow me."

Everyone followed him up the stairs. They went up to the second floor, and then up to the third floor. Yaoxing stopped in front of a room at the back of the third floor. Haiquan saw a round white bone plaque nailed above the door frame, with two small black characters "17" engraved on it. Yaoxing knocked on the door three times, and the door opened from the inside. Haiquan saw that there were already four or five people sitting inside. He had met two of them the previous two nights. He did not recognize three of them. He saw that the leader, Chen Huamin, had not yet arrived.

Thirty

Haiquan saw that the famous writer Li Yixiang, whom he admired, was wearing a gray cloth cotton robe, with his hands crossed into his sleeves, walking up and down the room, sometimes shaking his head, as if he was thinking about some kind of philosophy. He hurried up, respectfully called out Mr. Li, and then stretched out his right hand, asking to shake hands. Haiquan intentionally showed off to the two young people who came with him, showing that he knew the great writer Li Yixiang.

"Ah, Mr. Lin. You, you, why are you only coming now? You, you, young people, should be, be, be here earlier than, than, than us old predecessors!"

Although Li Yixiang gave Haiquan a lecture in an old-fashioned manner, he still shook hands with him warmly. After Haiquan shook hands with Li Yixiang, he went to ask the two young people he didn't recognize. He saw that one was dark-skinned, with a body as long and thin as a crane, and purple-black lips. Haiquan thought, this person must be smoking opium. The other was short, with hair more than a foot long, draped behind him. Haiquan thought, this is the characteristic of an artist.

After Haiquan displayed his social skills for a while, he retreated and sat next to Yaoxing, just about to ask Yaoxing why Chen Huamin hadn't come yet. But Yaoxing, without waiting for him to open his mouth, smiled and said to him:

"Why do you always put on such a pedantic appearance, like a pig dragging a dog!..."

Although Yaoxing was joking, he spoke loudly and aggressively. Haiquan blushed, secretly hating Tang Yaoxing's meanness. So he remembered what Mr. Zhu Weidao had said to him in the bus this morning.

"Old Tang, I heard you are going to have a conflict, Mr. Zhu Weidao, is that right?"

"Who said that?"
