After Retaking Huima Village

Enemy Advances and Reinforcements at Yu Pass 262

Infantry and Artillery Units Continuously Increase, Armored Vehicles Head to Shihe

Demanding Our Withdrawal from Shimen Village and Qin Island Defenses

Enemy Plans to Entirely Disrupt North China

Japanese Military Officer Publicly Declares Change of Plans

Enemy Fiercely Attacks Shanshen Temple in Lengkou Area, Repelled

(Beiping) Yesterday afternoon, Yu Pass saw an increase of four to five hundred Japanese soldiers, a combined force of infantry and artillery. There seems to be a continuous stream of reinforcements. A column of enemy armored vehicles has already advanced to Shihe to assist their infantry and cavalry in combat. According to Someya, the Japanese garrison commander on Qin Island, the Japanese military, having suffered defeats in battles at various passes along the Great Wall, intends to change its operational plan and attack Luodong. (30th Dispatch)

(Beiping) A Japanese Kwantung Army aircraft flew over Qin Island, dropping a communication to the Japanese camp. The content demanded that our army withdraw from the defensive structures at Shimen Village and Qin Island. Our battalion commander stationed on Qin Island, Liu Zhenying, has decided to ignore the demand and is actively preparing to resist. He has also requested that Mr. Chilton, a Briton, take note that the Japanese military should be responsible for all future losses in the war. (30th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Foreign dispatch: Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations has emboldened militarist arrogance. Many young officers of the Kwantung Army advocate for military action against Beiping and Tianjin, taking decisive measures and actively advancing troops. Key figures in the Japanese government have repeatedly issued wild pronouncements, vigorously promoting the theory of East Asian co-existence and co-prosperity, a change from the past pro-China-Japan rhetoric. They use this as an excuse to support a puppet state, hoping to conceal their intentions from international scrutiny. However, the Japanese government, parties, and business circles oppose the Japanese military entering the Guan region. (30th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yesterday morning, a certain unit of our army launched a counterattack and occupied the enemy position at Huimazhai, east of Shihe, killing over ten enemy soldiers. The enemy, unable to withstand the attack, retreated to Jiaoshan. Our army recaptured Huimazhai, seizing several enemy rifles and a large quantity of ammunition. Our army suffered five or six casualties. (30th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Kaiping Dispatch: At approximately 1:00 AM on the 29th, the enemy in front of Lengkou fiercely attacked the Xu battalion's position near Shanshen Temple, launching seven or eight assaults. Our army calmly met the attack, and the enemy was routed, suffering heavy casualties. Under the cover of firepower, they transported their corpses. We captured several bodies, as well as rifles, helmets, and other items, which are currently being inventoried. Our army suffered minor casualties and continues to hold the original position. On the same morning, several enemy aircraft dropped over ten bombs near our position, causing no damage. (30th Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to a certain military expert, the recent lull at various passes and the sudden increase in tension on the eastern front suggest that the enemy's intentions have shifted to encompass the entirety of North China. They aim to attack Qin Island and Yuluo to the east, and invade Chahar province to the west, creating a large encirclement targeting our area south of the Yellow River. Their first-stage military operations are north of the Great Wall, and the second stage are north of the Yellow River. This is evident from the military maps found on captured enemy soldiers by Song's forces. Now, their second-stage military operations have been launched against us, and our countrymen should be deeply alarmed. (29th Dispatch)

(Linyu) Since being ambushed and defeated by our army at Jiukou, the enemy has shown signs of increasing their numbers over the past few days, with frequent skirmishes between patrols from both sides. At approximately 6:00 AM on the 29th, about two hundred enemy soldiers, a mixed force of Japanese infantry, cavalry, and puppet troops, advanced from Shaguodian towards Qianshuiying. They were fiercely attacked by the defending soldiers of a certain regiment of our army. Simultaneously, a portion of a certain unit scaled the mountains to outflank the enemy, concentrating fire on them. The enemy gradually wavered. At approximately 7:00 AM, sixty to seventy enemy reinforcements moved towards our right flank from the Bai Guoshu heights, but our officers and soldiers calmly responded to the attack, using mortars and direct-fire artillery to engage them. By approximately 2:00 PM, over thirty Japanese soldiers rapidly advanced towards our position at Xiangshui, attempting to destroy our obstacles. They were met with intense fire from our army, suffering heavy casualties. The remaining enemy soldiers continued to resist in the area. By approximately 4:00 PM, the enemy at Qianshuiying could no longer withstand the attack and retreated along the entire line towards the Zhaojiayu area. Our army continues to hold the original position. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The fighting at Shimen Village has been fierce recently. The Japanese army dispatched a large unit from Yiyuan Pass as reinforcements, attempting to seize Shimen Village, leading to intense street fighting. The enemy first sent multiple bombers to indiscriminately drop bombs over Shimen Village and Qin Kong, many of which were incendiary bombs yesterday, causing most of the houses in the entire village to be destroyed by fire, with flames reaching the sky. Shimen Village will become the second Zhabei. (30th China United Press Dispatch)

(Beiping) North China currently feels peaceful, and the sense of security is gradually returning. However, the Chinese authorities still enforce a curfew from 11:00 PM to 5:00 AM the next morning. This morning, it was announced that the fronts at Lengkou, Xifengkou, Gubeikou, and Shihe were quiet yesterday. (30th Reuters Dispatch)

Reports on the Situation at the Front 263

(Nanjing) Xiao Zhenying, representative of Song Zheyuan, arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 30th to meet with Chiang Kai-shek, reporting on the situation of his army's operations at the front and seeking instructions. It is reported that the army has captured many war trophies from the enemy in this operation, taking over thirty photographs, which Xiao brought to Nanjing for printing and distribution to various sectors of society to allow the public to understand the reality of killing the enemy at the front and to boost morale. Song Zheyuan also telegraphed Nanjing to report on his army's recent annihilation of the enemy: (1) The enemy's Datun airfield was attacked by our militia and plainclothes teams on the night of the 27th, and five or six of their aircraft were burned. (2) On the afternoon of the 28th, a hundred or so enemy plainclothes soldiers disrupted our positions at Xifengkou and were repelled by our guerrillas. (3) The enemy at Gushanzi outside Dongjiakou and the enemy outside Tiemenguan have been severely attacked by our troops for days and have been routed towards Pingquan, thanks to our plainclothes units circling behind them. (30th Dispatch)

Central Executive Committee Resolution

National Congress to be Held on July 1st 265

National Assembly to be decided by the National Congress

Committee Member Wang Resigns as Premier; Request Difficult to Approve

Wang Jingwei Issues Statement

(Nanjing) At 8:00 AM on the 30th, the Central Committee held its 64th Standing Committee meeting. Fifty-three people were in attendance, including Yu Youren, Ye Chucang, Ju Zheng, Wang Zhaoming, Chiang Kai-shek, Gu Mengyu, Sun Ke, and Chen Guofu. Chiang Kai-shek chaired the meeting, which resolved the following important cases:

(1) The case of the Standing Committee's request to hold an interim National Congress on July 1st, 22nd year of the Republic, was resolved and passed.

(2) It was resolved that the Standing Committee believes the National Assembly should be convened ahead of schedule. This case should be submitted to the interim National Congress for discussion and decision.

(3) It was resolved that Committee Member Wang Zhaoming's resignation from the concurrent position of Premier of the Executive Yuan is difficult to approve, and he should resume his duties immediately.

(4) Amendment to Article 1000 of the Regulations on Rewarding Overseas Chinese Patriotic Donations.

(5) Recommended Committee Member Wu Chaoshu to report at the Central Memorial Week next Monday.

(6) Other routine cases. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) After the adjournment of the Central Standing Committee meeting, Wang told reporters, "Today's Central Standing Committee meeting resolved to hold an interim National Congress on July 1st of this year. This case was proposed by all the Standing Committee members. According to the Party Constitution, the National Congress is held every two years. The Fourth National Congress was held on December 12th, 20th year of the Republic. The Fifth National Congress should be convened on November 12th of this year. However, the Third Plenary Session last December resolved to convene a National Political Council on October 10th of this year and a National Assembly in the 24th year of the Republic. If the National Assembly can be convened ahead of schedule, then there is no need to convene the National Political Council again. According to the Outline of National Reconstruction, local self-government should be completed before the National Assembly is convened. Currently, the date for the National Assembly is only a little over a year away. The government has a mountain of cases concerning the promotion of local self-government, but due to economic constraints, it cannot complete local self-government by the 24th year of the Republic. Therefore, all members of the Central Standing Committee believe that it is better to convene the National Assembly ahead of schedule. Whether the National Political Council should be convened as scheduled on October 10th of this year, or whether the National Assembly should be convened ahead of schedule this year, this matter must be decided by the National Congress. Furthermore, the legally mandated time for the Fifth National Congress is after the National Political Council. Therefore, today's Central Standing Committee resolved to convene an interim National Congress on July 1st to decide whether the National Political Council should be convened as scheduled, or whether the National Assembly should be convened ahead of schedule. As for whether the Fifth National Congress still needs to be held or whether it should be postponed, and whether the Central Committee members should be re-elected by the interim National Congress or by the Fifth National Congress, these will also be decided by the interim National Congress. In addition, the case of open governance proposed by Li Liejun has also been submitted to the interim National Congress for discussion. As for whether the Central Committee needs to hold a plenary meeting before the convening of the interim National Congress, this matter was also mentioned in today's Standing Committee meeting, and it was generally believed that there was no need to convene one." (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Issue of Japan's Mandated Islands 267

Will Germany Seek Compromise with Japan?

Berlin Dispatch: Regarding the issue of returning the South Pacific Islands, the German government will formally negotiate after the arrival of Japanese Ambassador to Germany, Nagai. Preliminary negotiations were recently held in secret by German Social Democratic Party leader and Minister of Propaganda Goebbels, Foreign Ministry Information Director Finke, Foreign Minister Loringberk, other diplomatic figures, and the Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Fujii. According to reliable reports, the German side put forward the following views in the meeting: (1) Germany recognizes that the South Pacific Islands have no economic or colonial value for present-day Germany. (2) According to the Four-Power Pact proposed by MacDonald, the colonial issue will also come to the fore. In this context, the German National Socialist Party (Nazi Party) publicly advocates the return of Germany's former colonies, and the South Pacific issue will also be linked to it. (3) For the sake of appearances, Japan cannot return the South Pacific Islands to the Allies. It would be better to take the form of returning them to Germany. (4) The South Pacific Islands are of absolute military importance to Japan, which Germany fully understands. Therefore, Germany will not infringe on Japan's rights in the various facilities on the South Pacific Islands. (5) The two sides may be able to find a compromise whereby the South Pacific Islands are entrusted to Japan for military use in substance, while formally returning them to Germany.

Geneva Dispatch: According to general observation, the purpose of Germany's expression of demanding the return of the South Pacific Islands is merely to establish a principle for the return of former territories. Germany's true focus is not on the South Pacific Islands but on other former colonies. As for France, it opposes the return of the South Pacific Islands to Germany, as this would give Germany an excuse to expand its navy. (World Press)

(Berlin) The "Deutsche Tageszeitung" commented today on Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the status of the Pacific mandated islands, saying that Germany, in any case, does not wish to clash with Japan. It hopes that after open and friendly discussions, Japan's concerns can be dispelled and anti-German propaganda can be stopped. At the same time, Germans must deny that the mandated islands are genuine spoils of war from former enemies and insist that the League of Nations has the right to supervise the legal status of the mandated territories. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Japanese Ships Suspend Service One After Another 271

Affected by Anti-Japanese Sentiment

The Osaka Asahi Shimbun reported on the 24th that since the anti-Japanese movement in various parts of China, the shipping business of Japanese ships has been declining daily. Vessels connecting central and northern China, such as the Dalian Kisen Kaisha's Tianjin Maru, which departed from Shanghai on March 5th, and the Kawasaki Kisen Kaisha's Shirozaki Maru, which departed from Tianjin on March 10th, were the last routes. In the future, these routes will inevitably be monopolized by the British Taikoo Company, the British Jardine Matheson & Co., and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. In short, due to the anti-Japanese movement, Japanese ships have repeatedly suspended service, hindering business, which is regrettable. However, the situation in the Chinese interior is comparatively different. For example, in Shandong, due to negotiations with local officials, anti-Japanese sentiment is outwardly promoted, but it has not been affected in any way in reality. Transactions are still carried out as usual, so imports of Japanese goods have been quite prosperous for a time. However, trade in the Tianjin and Beiping areas has been relatively sluggish recently.

He arrived in Nagasaki on the Shanghai Maru on the 31st and made the following remarks on the situation of Chinese trade: "The boycott of Japanese goods is still ongoing. However, practical commodities, no matter how suppressed, have gradually opened up their position. Foreigners who do not handle Japanese goods also need more and more Japanese goods. Recently, two large-scale Japanese department stores have been opened in the French Concession. By changing the packaging style and brand, the sales performance is excellent. As for the anti-Japanese sentiment of the Chinese people, it cannot be changed in a day or two, so we should make special efforts in this regard."

All four abducted crew members were British: one was Second Engineer Bairu, one was Third Engineer Peirce, one was Johnson, and one was Hargrave. The latter two were junior crew members. Captain Law-Pinson rushed to the radio room to send an alert, but the radio operator was not in the room. He returned to his cabin to get a weapon, but by that time the pirates had already taken the four crew members far away. The pirates' small boat escaped into shallow water, so the steamer, which drew more water, could not follow. A British gunboat has now joined the search for the pirates' small boat. German Nazis Retaliate 274

Boycott Movement Spreads Nationwide

Reuters, Berlin, 29th: Prime Minister Hitler stated in today's cabinet meeting that he would implement a boycott against Jews on April 1st. According to news from London, an organized movement to boycott German goods is underway there. Jews in New York are also working hard to incite all kinds of Americans. When the National Socialist Party announces the implementation of the boycott against Jews, the German government will implement countermeasures to avoid acts of violence. Overseas Jews should know that if Jews wage war against Germany, the German Jews will suffer the most. German Jews are naturally trembling at the boycott on April 1st and are trying their best to get it cancelled. This boycott will leave tens of thousands of Jews in ruin and will leave hundreds of thousands of Christians who serve Jews in a difficult position. Therefore, the people of Germany now hope that the "propaganda of abuse" made overseas will be stopped immediately, and then the National Socialist Party can cancel the boycott. Hitler did not say that the entire German government did not approve of this move, and of course major bankers did not support it either. The boycott against Jews began today and is rapidly spreading throughout the country.

Havas, Berlin, 29th: Since the National Socialist Party issued a proclamation calling for a boycott of Jews, a Central Boycott Committee has been established here to investigate the addresses of Jewish merchants, doctors, and lawyers, and to specify the types of goods that should be boycotted. This boycott is expected to be implemented in an organized manner throughout Germany starting on Saturday. The boycott has already begun in many places. In the city of Münster in Westphalia, members of the National Socialist Party are guarding the doors of 48 Jewish shops and occupying the court, expelling all Jewish lawyers. In the city of Dortmund, under the pretext of protection, a large number of Jews were arrested. In the city of Görlitz, members of the National Socialist Party are guarding the entrance to the court, carrying out inspections. The presiding judge, two lawyers, and many others were arrested and will be imprisoned. The mayor of Frankfurt am Main has ordered that all Jewish civil servants in the municipal government be dismissed. However, there have been no bloodshed incidents in any place.

Bread Shortage in Soviet Russia 277

Famine Throughout Kazakhstan

Report of a British Man's Visit to Russia

Reuters, Berlin, 29th: Mr. Kennet, the former political secretary of Lloyd George, has returned to England after walking and inspecting Soviet Russia. He has now arrived in Berlin. According to him, there is currently a widespread famine in Soviet Russia, just like the great famine of 1921. Millions of people have already died of starvation alone. There are cries of "We have no bread and will starve to death" everywhere in Soviet Russia. It is said that one million people have starved to death in the Kazakhstan region, because there is not enough seed there, and most of the farmers are too weak to plow. Kennet believes that the cause of the famine is due to farmers resisting the government's collectivization of land, and the lack of skilled workers and the collapse of economic transportation. Kennet also said that the case of the six British engineers arrested by the Vickers Electrical Company and the shooting of 35 farmer leaders were all actions to appease the people. Previously, Kennet had expressed sympathy for the Soviet Union's experiments and had spent six years inspecting various parts of the Soviet Union. It is shocking to hear him suddenly give such a report about Soviet Russia.

Wreckage of British Airplane

The Tragedy of the Victims 293

Reuters, Dixmuide, 29th - The British airplane "City of Liverpool," deeply embedded in the soil with smoldering remains, was being excavated by workers all day today to a depth reaching the waist, in order to retrieve the remains of the thirteen victims. The work proceeded slowly. Initially, it was anticipated that only five bodies could be transferred to the coroner's office today, but by evening, all thirteen terribly gruesome bodies had been exhumed and identified. Three bodies were missing their heads, and two had their arms intertwined. After the bodies were removed, three French airplanes flew over the crash site and dropped wreaths. According to reports, the "City of Liverpool" carried a total of fifteen people, including thirteen passengers and two crew members. Shortly after flying into Belgian territory, the plane suddenly caught fire, and everyone on board perished. However, two people were farther from the plane's wreckage, likely having jumped out before the fuselage landed. Among the fifteen victims, eleven were British, three were German, and one was Belgian.

Reuters, London, 29th - Sir Sassoon, Under-Secretary of State for Air, stated in the House of Commons today that all seats on today's flight to Paris were fully booked, and many people who bought tickets were unable to get on. This proves that yesterday's crash of the "City of Liverpool" in Belgium has not shaken public confidence in Imperial Airways. Regarding news of the "City of Liverpool" crash, no further reports are available at this time. However, it should be noted that Imperial Airways airplanes have not had an accident in two and a half years, during which they have flown four million miles and carried 99,000 passengers. Airplanes of the "City of Liverpool" type have been commonly used for the past six years.

The Japanese Collapse Theory in the Eyes of the British (Continued) 296

Translated from the Manchester Guardian

The possibility of controlling the Japanese yen by reducing imports and increasing exports is very weak. This is a continuous cycle, and inflation is therefore more certain. The extent of inflation depends on the government's ability to raise funds from the people or banks. Judging from the financial strength of various commercial banks, there is still some collateral for borrowing. Japan is indeed willing to make great sacrifices for the sake of invading other countries and imperialist expansion. Even so, the budget situation and the deficit in foreign exchange balance will probably be worse in the coming months than before. Without foreign economic assistance, it will be difficult for Japan to maintain its current military spending.

Since around July of last year, inflation has been evident, such as rising prices, inconsistencies in the fluctuations of various commodity prices, a further sharp decline in the exchange rate of the Japanese yen, and a significant increase in the cost of living. The general wholesale price index has increased by more than 15 percent in the last three months, while the retail price index has increased by 6 percent. The Bank of Japan's cost-of-living index increased by 7.5 percent between July and October. Wages do not seem to have increased, but there are no recent statistics available. If the price of rice had not fallen sharply due to an unprecedented bumper harvest since March 1932, the cost of living would undoubtedly have increased much more. However, although the price of rice fell by 20 percent between February and October, the price of wheat rose by 35 percent, the price of cotton yarn rose by 55 percent, the price of steel rose by more than 50 percent, and the price of raw silk rose by 90 percent from its lowest point in June to October, half of which was due to the poor silk cocoon harvest. The number of registered unemployed was 439,000 in October 1931 and increased to 482,000 in June 1932. This is the last survey result, but it may decrease afterward, because in recent months, industry and commerce have been temporarily encouraged and seduced by inflation.

Cotton yarn exports in September of last year were 3.1 percent higher than in October 1931, cotton fabric production was 7.9 percent higher, and silk fabric (including rayon) production was 31.2 percent higher. However, the increase in overall industrial production (twelve main commodities) was only about 2.5 percent, because the production of other commodities was low. The fall in the price of rice has greatly affected farmers who are already heavily in debt. Although the Japanese Parliament decided in September to allocate relief funds of about 300 million yen annually, only one-third of this money will reach the hands of farmers. The rest is designated for the relief of the Central and local Industrial Banks. The position of the local Industrial Banks is very unstable, and private commercial banks also have a strong exterior but weak interior. Both deposits and loans, especially the investment portion of loans, have continued to decline since September 1931. This tense situation was temporarily eased in the first half of 1932 after the abandonment of the gold standard, and the issuance of cash in proportion to debt repayment can still stabilize people's minds.

Export-Import Gap

In the first nine months of 1932, the total value of Japanese (including Korea, Taiwan, and Ryukyu) imports was approximately 1,005.4 million yen, excluding fractions, while the total value of exports was approximately 938 million yen. Compared to the same period in 1931, the total value of imports increased by 89 million, and the total value of exports increased by 49 million. Therefore, the visible trade deficit increased from 76 million to 116 million. However, these increased figures are all virtual, and are actually due to the depreciation of the Japanese yen. Calculated in gold prices, the total value of imports in the first nine months of 1931 was US$51.2 million, which fell to US$33.9 million in the same period of 1932, while the total value of exports fell from US$45.4 million to US$29.2 million. Therefore, the visible trade deficit fell from US$5.8 million to US$4.7 million. The export volume of cotton fabrics has greatly increased, almost doubling in 1932. However, the average export price of cotton fabrics, calculated in gold prices, was US$106 per thousand yards in 1929 (equivalent to 230 yen), which fell to US$35 (equivalent to 147 yen) by last September, a decrease of almost two-thirds. This shows that the reduction in commodity prices is partly the result of Japanese commodity dumping, because when the price of the Japanese yen fell sharply, the gold price of Japanese cotton goods fell more than that of other countries. During the same period, the export price of cotton fabrics from the British Commonwealth, calculated in gold prices, fell by less than 50 percent.

Regarding the latest figures for the export-import gap, visible and invisible, it is difficult to obtain them, but based on logical deduction, there are fears of an unfavorable panic soon. The price of Japanese bonds in foreign markets has been sluggish for several months, which is a sign of this concern. In the last three months of 1932, there may be some major changes in the visible export-import gap. The first step of the expansionary policy may encourage exports more than imports, and it is natural that Japan's foreign trade will have a favorable visible gap in the second half of last year.

Unfavorable Main Reasons

However, contrary to this possibility, there are several other main reasons, which will be briefly discussed. These include the increase in external debt calculated in foreign currency and the increase in interest payments in Japanese yen, which will definitely be a heavy blow to the budget. The reduction in income from Japanese investment in Manchuria and other parts of China, the reduction in profits from shipping and tourism to Japan, the huge military spending and Japanese diplomatic expenses abroad, the reduction in borrowing long-term or short-term capital from foreign countries, and continued investment in Manchuria, the number of gold reserves is extremely small, requiring great difficulty to transport goods again. The Bank of Japan's gold reserves were 83.1 million yen at the end of January 1931, and 81.7 million at the end of September of the same year. Since then, gold reserves have decreased, reaching only 42.8 million yen by the end of November last year.

Moreover, although the development of manufacturing industry will definitely continue due to the increase in exports, there are also restrictions. Because of currency depreciation, in terms of cost, more Japanese yen can be obtained when selling, but imported raw materials must be paid for with depreciated Japanese yen. This benefit is limited by this fact. Therefore, the net profit, in addition to the further depreciation of the Japanese yen from the time of import to the time of export, lies in the difference between the domestic production cost (such as interest and wages) and the amount of Japanese yen obtained at the time of sale. When the increasing cost of living forces wages to rise, this difference will disappear.

Two new gold producing areas have indeed been discovered in Japan, and have recently attracted attention from certain parties. These two places are actually placer gold producing areas, and their locations have become famous for a while, and may not provide much help to the improvement of Japan's financial situation. Based on the facts mentioned above regarding Japan's financial and economic situation, it can be known that it is difficult for Japan to stand in a position of confrontation with the rest of the world, and it is also ineffective to seek understanding from European powers for intervention in the Manchurian Incident.

Kong Xiangxi Returns to Shanghai This Morning 297

Discussing His Inspection of the Northern Front Lines and

Stating His Willingness to Undertake Anti-Japanese Work

Chairman Chiang to Visit Shanghai in the Middle of the 1st and 2nd

Kong Xiangxi, Special Envoy for the Inspection of European and American Industries, returned to the country from Europe and immediately reported his findings to the Central Government in Nanjing. He then went north to Beiping and Tianjin, and to Xifengkou to comfort the anti-Japanese soldiers led by Song Zheyuan and others. He also went to Baoding to meet with Chiang, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission. He returned south a few days ago, arriving in Shanghai this morning at 8:00 AM on the overnight train from Nanjing, accompanied by his wife, Madame Soong Ai-ling. According to Kong this morning speaking to reporters of this newspaper, Chiang Kai-shek is scheduled to visit Shanghai around the 1st or 2nd of the month. Today, due to other important official business in Nanjing, he may not have time to leave. Regarding the requests from various parties to appoint Chiang as Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, Kong believes that under the current circumstances, it is necessary to establish such a position in order to unify military power and facilitate command. His remarks are recorded as follows:

Inspection of Xifengkou 298

Kong stated first that, on this trip north to meet with Chairman Chiang, he made a special trip to Xifengkou to inspect the front lines of our army and comfort the anti-Japanese soldiers led by Song Zheyuan and others. He repeatedly met with generals such as Song Zheyuan and Pang Bingxun. The defensive works of our army are exceptionally solid, and morale is extremely high. Regarding food and equipment, the Central Government is providing as much assistance as possible, so there is no need to worry about shortages. Currently, the military situation in Xifengkou is in a stalemate. Song Zheyuan's troops and others are bravely fighting the enemy, and their contributions are extremely significant. Our side has also suffered heavy casualties.

Japanese Air of Appeasement 299

Kong continued, stating that after each military action, the Japanese are sure to spread various rumors in an attempt to soften the atmosphere. In reality, this is entirely a deceptive tactic. Their ambition to gain an inch and then seek a mile has never changed. In the future, they will undoubtedly resume their ferocious face and plot a large-scale invasion again. There is absolutely no doubt about this. The Central Government has made thorough preparations for the military situation in North China and is determined to fight the enemy to the end. Rumors of compromise and direct negotiations with Japan are completely unfounded. In today's situation, compromising with Japan is an act of either being insane or devoid of conscience.

Chairman Chiang's Visit to Shanghai 300

Kong added that after returning to Nanjing, he repeatedly met with Chairman Chiang. He heard that Chiang would visit Shanghai around the 1st or 2nd of the month, and then go north again to oversee the situation. However, due to other important official business in Nanjing today, he may not have time to come here. It has not yet been decided whether he will travel by train or airplane. As for Zhang Xueliang in Shanghai, he heard that he has recently been suffering from a minor illness. He plans to visit him soon.

Issue of Commander-in-Chief 301

Reporters immediately inquired about the widespread telegrams to the government from various sectors, requesting the appointment of Chairman Chiang as Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, asking whether this could be realized. Kong replied that he had not returned to the country for long and did not know the specifics of this case. However, speaking not from a personal viewpoint, under today's circumstances, in order to unify military power and facilitate command, it is necessary to establish a Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force.

Undertaking Anti-Japanese Work 302

Kong also stated that he is currently organizing the findings of his recent inspection in Europe and America. He will make them public in their entirety in the future. Reporters then asked whether he would continue to be responsible for the work of revitalizing industry and commerce. He replied that in today's perilous national situation, when we are teetering on the brink of disaster, talking about revitalizing industry is too slow to be of immediate help. He is extremely willing to undertake anti-Japanese work and fulfill his responsibility as a citizen to save the country.

Opposition to Dictatorship 303

Finally, regarding the issue of dictatorship, reporters asked whether today's China, like Germany under Hitler and Italy under Mussolini, could be revived through dictatorship. Kong replied that China's problem today is not one of system, but of people. Dictatorship is good, but who can implement it? There are many different opinions, and government orders are inconsistent. The rise of a thing, arguments arise, all doing work on the text, and very little is seen in facts. He sincerely hopes that the people of the country will unite and work hard to resist foreign aggression, otherwise the country will perish imminently, and what system can be discussed? Kong expressed his feelings with great emotion.

Three Major Ceremonies at Jiaotong University 304

Opening Ceremony Held at the Engineering Building and Rong Hong Hall

Industrial and Railway Exhibition Held Simultaneously

The 37th anniversary of National Jiaotong University, the Industrial and Railway Exhibition held this morning at the Wen Zhi Hall opening ceremony, and simultaneously also hold the Engineering Hall opening ceremony, Rong Hong Hall Completion Ceremony, starting at 9 o'clock, until noon before scattering, now will be the circumstances described below,

Representatives and Guests 305

Starting at 9 o'clock this morning, Consuls from various countries, government representatives, representatives from various schools, and Chinese and foreign guests arrived at the school one after another to visit and participate in various ceremonies. These included German Acting Consul-General in Shanghai, Beinert, Vice-Consul Moore, Swedish Consul-General Lalan, National Government and Shanghai Municipal Government representative Yu Hongjun, Railway Department Minister Gu's representative Xia Guangyu, Industry Department representative Liu Yinfol, Education Department Minister Zhu's representative Wu Shuwei, former Deputy Minister of Industry Zhao Jinqing, Municipal Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan, Municipal Public Works Bureau Director Xu Peihuang, Jiangsu Provincial Government representative Xu Xingcheng, Songhu Garrison Headquarters representative Xu Yiheng, Naval Training Ship Staff Officer Wu Guanghai, Public Security Bureau representative Huang Zuna, Beiping Railway Administration Zeng Zhaoyi, Two Roads Bureau Traffic Department Director Zheng Baozhao, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau Fan Shouzhi, Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau Cheng Kaogang, Shanghai Law College Chu Fucheng, Nanjing Central University Liu Qifeng, and Tongji University Weng Zilong, among hundreds of others.

Engineering Hall Opening 306

The Engineering Hall opening ceremony was held at 9:00 AM in front of the Engineering Hall. First, Dean Li gave a report, stating in brief that the construction of the Engineering Hall was proposed in the 15th year of the Republic, raising only 30,000 yuan in construction funds. It was delayed until the 19th year, when Railway Minister Sun Zhesheng, who headed the school, enthusiastically promoted industrial construction, and the old proposal was brought up again and actively carried out. Construction began in February of the 20th year and was completed at the end of the year. The entire hall occupies an area of 4,200 square feet, with a volume of 42,000 cubic feet, divided into two floors. The lower floor is for laboratories and factories, and the upper floor is for research, surveying, and classrooms. In the future, if expansion is needed, another floor can be added on top, as this was prepared for during the design and construction. After the report, architect Wu handed over the key and wished for engineering progress and industrial development. Dean Hu received the key and unlocked it. Dean Zhang continued to speak, saying that he was deeply gratified that the hall had been completed through the efforts of President Li. Looking back on the school's founding, it has focused on civil engineering from the beginning, but all the equipment was very rudimentary. Two or three years later, a flat roof was added to the existing electrical machinery factory and instruments were added, which was the beginning of the electrical engineering hall. Over the decades, various equipment has been added, but it is far inferior to today. However, successive graduates have either served in government agencies, working on political, transport and other work, or have used their own experience to start industries, all with outstanding achievements. Even in this exhibition, the diesel engine of Xinzhong Engineering Company, the transformer of Yizhong Electrical Machinery Company, and the radio equipment of Wireless Research Company and Sanji Rui Electrical Company are all the result of the efforts of the school's alumni. Now that we have such superior equipment, we should redouble our efforts. England's Grans Building Laboratory, which was established in 1915, led to the invention of the steam engine, the ancestor of today's prime movers. The Royal School of England built the Taytes Laboratory, which led to Faraday's discovery of electromagnetic induction in 1831. Therefore, I have endless hopes for the completion of the Engineering Hall.

Rong Hong Hall Completed 307

The Rong Hong Hall completion ceremony was held at 9:30 AM in front of the Rong Hong Hall. First, Dean Zhao gave a report, saying that in recent years, the number of courses has increased, and the number of students has also increased, resulting in insufficient allocation of school buildings. When Sun was president of the school, he had a five-year and ten-year plan, and the construction of Rong Hong Hall was also part of the plan. Solicitation began in July of last year, bidding in August, and construction began in September, and it was completed in March of this year. The entire hall occupies an area of 1,949 square feet and has three floors, used as offices for the management department. After the report, architect Zhuang assisted the key and wished for the development of school affairs and the prosperity of the country. Engineer Rong received the key and unlocked it, and then President Li gave a speech, saying that the school's building was to commemorate the worthy predecessor Rong Hong, so not only to leave a memorial in material terms, but also to get a good lesson in spirit. A hundred years ago, Rong Hong advocated innovation and suggested ten items to Li Hongzhang. The creation of the school is also due to this, and the 120 students who were sent abroad at that time made a great contribution to the reform-minded China in the decades that followed. Rong Hong's vision and advocacy were all based on patriotism. We built this Rong Hong Hall to commemorate him, hoping that students will work hard to complete his unfinished will.

Exhibition Opens 308

The opening ceremony of the Industrial and Railway Exhibition was held at the Wen Zhi Hall at 10:00 AM. First, Hu Ruixing, director of the preparatory committee, gave a report, saying that the school has had large-scale exhibitions twice. The first time was in the 5th year of the Republic, when the school celebrated its 20th anniversary, and the second time was when the school celebrated its 30th anniversary. In the 35th year of the Republic two years ago, the Industrial and Railway Exhibition was planned, but due to the 918 and 128 incidents, the national crisis suddenly arose, so it was postponed. At the end of last year, preparations were started again, and after many meetings in April, it was finally able to open, which is very gratifying. The exhibition is also divided into two types: Type A, which is given by various parties, and Type B, which is displayed. There are 12 exhibitors in the railway, 60 manufacturers, 9 schools, and 6 agencies. Foreign manufacturers include 33 from the United Kingdom, 28 from Germany, 26 from Belgium, 14 from the United States, 14 from Switzerland, 7 from France, 4 from Italy, 3 from Canada, and 1 each from Sweden, Hungary, Denmark, Russia, and the Netherlands. Xia Guangyu, representative of the Railway Department Minister Gu, said in his speech that Jiaotong University is well-managed, well-equipped, and has been expanded and improved by successive presidents. The talents it has cultivated have all served in society and have achieved excellent results. Therefore, it occupies an important position in the process of building a new China. The significance of the Industrial and Railway Exhibition is also very significant: (1) To provide an opportunity for the study of academic theory and the needs of practice to be explored, and to make a comparison of domestic and foreign industries; (2) To arouse the attention of the Chinese people to industry. In today's country, if we want to survive, we must work hard to build it. Therefore, the strength of the country depends on the thickness of the national production capacity. Since the rise of the machine industry, industry has been trending towards the end, but our country still does not pay attention to the construction of industry. This is also an important reason why the country is getting weaker day by day. Although various raw materials can be produced by ourselves, the Industrial and Railway Exhibition cannot be manufactured, so it is important to promote the attention of the Chinese people, especially during this national crisis. Yu Hongjun, representative of the National Government and the Municipal Government, gave a speech, saying that Jiaotong University has a glorious history, great achievements, and has made even greater contributions to the new construction. Holding the Industrial and Railway Exhibition during the current national crisis has great significance. The weakness of our country's industry, commerce, and transportation is one of the reasons. The reason for the underdevelopment of industry lies in the fact that the Chinese people do not pay attention to scientific management. Some people even think that imitating the 19th-century British efforts in domestic industry can also develop. Sun Yat-sen's instruction, capital is machinery, shows that large-scale production using machinery is not enough to talk about industry. Therefore, this exhibition, in addition to making the Chinese people aware of machinery, also hopes to emphasize the significance of scientific management. Then Education Department representative Wu Shuwei and others gave speeches, and it did not end until noon.

Post Office Announcement

Returning Savings from the Liaoning Area 311

The Shanghai Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau has issued an announcement this morning regarding the return of fixed deposit receipts from the Liaoning area:

Announcement: It has been verified that all depositors within the territory of the three northeastern provinces who hold savings books or fixed deposit receipts issued by various bureaus in the Liaoning postal area before July 23, 1932, and in the Jilin-Heilongjiang postal area before July 25, 1932, must register with the bureau in person or through their agent. The registration methods are detailed below:

(1) Savings books for passbook savings can be registered at any post office (excluding branches) within the country that handles passbook savings. Fixed deposit receipts for fixed deposits should be registered at post offices (excluding branches) that handle fixed deposits.

(2) If the depositor intends to leave the savings in the post office, a new savings book or new fixed deposit receipt will be issued by the registering post office one month after the registration date. For savings originally deposited in Harbin dollars in the Jilin-Heilongjiang postal area—that is, if the savings book or deposit receipt does not specify silver dollars—they will be converted into silver dollars at 80% of their value. Interest on these retained savings will be calculated from the day after the last day of interest calculation in the three northeastern provinces (i.e., June 30, 1932). Interest on fixed deposits will be calculated from the original deposit date at the original interest rate.

(3) If the depositor wishes to withdraw these savings, they must also wait one month from the registration date and then, following usual procedures, submit a withdrawal slip to the original registering bureau, along with the savings book or fixed deposit receipt, to withdraw the savings. All withdrawal slips and fixed deposit receipts must be signed and sealed with the original seal of the depositor. The interest on all withdrawn savings will be calculated according to the method described in Section 2 above, up to the date of registration.

(4) The post office may, if deemed necessary, request the depositor to provide a reliable guarantor before returning the savings.

(5) All savings return transactions will be handled at the original registering bureau. If the original savings were deposited in Harbin dollars (see Section 2 above), they will be returned converted into silver dollars at 80% of their value.

All the above sections are hereby announced for general information.

Postal Director Zha Peilin

Social Affairs Bureau

Expanding Agricultural Cooperation Experiment Zone 312

Adding Pengpu and Jiangwan Districts

The agricultural cooperation experiment zone established by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau in recent years has achieved remarkable results and is well-received by farmers. Last year, due to the war, the Yinheng, Zhenru, and Pusong districts could not be implemented. The bureau has recently drafted an expansion plan. In addition to restoring the Yinheng, Zhenru, and Pusong districts, it will also add the Pengpu and Jiangwan districts. The general situation of the experiment zone last year and the expansion plan for the 21st year are recorded below:

Last Year’s Harvest in Each District Last year, the experiment zone established by the bureau included Yangsi, Luhang, Caojing, Gaohang, Fahua, Tangqiao, and Yangjing districts. The Yangsi district was divided into 18 units, with a total harvest of 5,790 catties. The Luhang district was divided into 12 units, with a total harvest of 6,550 catties. The Caojing district was divided into 6 units, with a total harvest of 2,383 catties. The Gaohang district was divided into 6 units, with a total harvest of 2,415 catties. The Fahua district was divided into 6 units, with a total harvest of 1,552 catties. The Tangqiao district had 12 units, with a total harvest of 6,505 catties. The Yangjing district was divided into 6 units, with a total harvest of 2,265 catties.

Plan for the 21st Year The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau’s agricultural cooperation experiment zone plan for the 21st year:

(1) Location: In addition to the seven districts of Luhang, Yangsi, Tangqiao, Caojing, Gaohang, Fahua, and Yangjing, which should be implemented successively, the Yinheng, Zhenru, and Pusong districts should also be restored to achieve results. Furthermore, the Pengpu and Jiangwan districts should be added to promote popularization.

(2) Organization: The bureau will entrust municipal committee members and farmers' associations in each district to select excellent local farmers and establish units in appropriate locations. The farmers will be responsible for management and will be guided and supervised by the bureau, the municipal committees in each district, and the farmers' associations. A supervisor may be hired as needed, but without salary.

(3) Facilities: This year, the experiment will still be limited to cotton cultivation. Twelve units will be established in the Xuhang, Yangsi, and Tangqiao districts, divided into two zones. The remaining nine districts will each have six units, for a total of ninety units.

(4) Subsidies: Each unit is allocated five mu of level land, with an experimental fee of three silver dollars per mu. Each district will also receive a supervisor's travel allowance of forty-five yuan and a seed fee of fifteen yuan.

Abolition of the Civil Service Appointment Regulations 313

The Municipal Government received Instruction No. 1178 from the Executive Yuan yesterday, stating that Instruction No. 82 of the National Government has abolished the Civil Service Appointment Regulations, and Instruction No. 3 states that the Civil Service Law has been enacted and officially promulgated. Upon receiving this, all subordinate agencies should be informed accordingly. After receiving the order, the Municipal Government immediately copied the original text and issued it to all subordinate agencies for compliance.

Opening of the Trial for the Case of Maternal Uncle Abducting and Selling His Niece 314

Gui Bao, the thirteen-year-old daughter of Wang Le, a Ningbo woman residing at No. 46 Zhaofeng Road, was studying in the evening class at the nearby Muyi Christian School for two hours. On the afternoon of December 21st last year, at 7:00 PM, she went to the school to study but never returned. There was no news. Until February of this year, her mother, Zhang Le, learned in her hometown that Gui Bao had been abducted and sold by her son, Wenxing, in collusion with Gong Li, Chai Lu, Li Liu, and other Ningbo women residing at No. 147 Aierkao Ke Road, No. 38 Dongyouheng Road, etc., to a wealthy man in the Xinghua County of Fujian Province. They received three hundred silver dollars and divided the spoils for their own use. The mother was furious, considering it an unprecedented act of a maternal uncle abducting and selling his niece. She beat him severely and made him write down the addresses of each woman. She then came to Shanghai and informed her daughter, Wang Le, who reported it to the Huishan Police Station. Detective Li Hongsheng was dispatched to secretly arrest the three women at their addresses and send them to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. Details have been reported in this newspaper. This morning, Judge Wu Gang and Judge Han presided over the continued interrogation in the Third Criminal Court. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu of the police station stated the previous circumstances and also said that, according to investigations during the interim period, the defendant Gong Li was actually not involved and requested her release. A letter has now been received from the Ningbo County Government, stating that Le Wenxing had already fled without a trace on the 21st of this month upon hearing the news. The letter was presented for inspection. Wang Le then explained the details of the incident, and her mother, Zhang Le, testified that she had entrusted relatives to watch over Le Wenxing at the time, but he had escaped and she did not know where he was staying. Chai Lu testified that although she had previously been acquainted with Le Wenxing, they had separated last September due to differences and were not involved in the abduction. She asked for leniency. Li Liu testified that she had known Le Wenxing as a neighbor, and he had repeatedly tried to seduce her but failed, making false accusations. Judge Wu ordered them to be remanded in custody for sentencing at a later date, and Gong Li was granted release.

Page 21

Talks

Shanghai's National Crisis 315

— Wu

Since September 18th, our China has suddenly faced a "national crisis." Since the nation is already in "crisis," it should be very painful. This can be seen from the government's repeated orders for "the whole country to lower flags at half-mast in mourning." It can be seen that the government attaches great importance to and is enthusiastic about the "national crisis." It seems that no matter how calm, the two words "national crisis" are always shouted out first. And we, the common people, because it is "justified," boldly follow suit and shout even louder.

In Shanghai, the call for "national crisis" is, of course, even more lively. For a long time, many patriotic comrades had black gauze wrapped around their sleeves, and the four white characters "Together to Face the National Crisis" were printed on them. How passionate, how "patriotic, not daring to lag behind." Later, the January 28th Incident occurred, and Shanghai was truly in "national crisis." Many people with no money and no weapons were slaughtered and burned by Japanese imperialism, resulting in wives and children being separated, and families being destroyed. Because they had no possibility of moving and had not received orders that the people could also resist with arms, the English and American flags fluttered on the cars of the masters and mistresses, and they had already called servants, and moved the whole family to the concession, including opium pipes and foreign dogs. After listening to the gramophone record of "Foreigners Laughing" and four rounds of mahjong, they also dressed neatly and went up to the roof garden to listen to the distant sounds of gunfire or watch the fire with binoculars, to show that they did not forget the "national crisis." Later, the National Army retreated to Zhenru in accordance with orders. After it was written in the May 5th Agreement that China could not station troops in Shanghai, some people squeezed a cold sweat, and some ran to the scorched earth and rubble to dig for the white bones of their wives, children, and parents, while the masters and mistresses thanked God and laughed with joy. At this time, the national crisis in Shanghai had naturally passed. Naturally, in the dance halls, in the wine shops, in the massage parlors, in the racecourses, the so-called "national crisis" had long disappeared without a trace. Naturally, it was a celebration for all, and the world was at peace.

However, even though "dancing to save the country" and "entertainment to save the country" are now shouted with all their might, "aviation to save the country" has followed, rising and resounding through the clouds. It can be seen that the people of Shanghai are still very interested in the "national crisis." At least because this kind of "saving the country" is not so troublesome. All that is needed is for everyone to take out money to decorate the "national crisis." Moreover, it is said that this kind of "saving the country" is the most effective.

The best thing is that the sounds of horses neighing and people shouting north of the Great Wall, and the planes and cannons on the edge of Rehe, cannot be heard at all in Shanghai. Even if thousands of Chinese soldiers in the guise of peasants are killed, it is still irrelevant to Shanghai. In addition, there are rumors of direct negotiations, and Japanese imperialism will certainly not attack Shanghai again. Therefore, being so enthusiastic about "saving the country" as it is now is indeed sufficient and more than enough.

However, there are also some people who want another war to happen in Shanghai, because, as in the January 28th Incident, a pavilion room can get a rent of twenty yuan, which is indeed a rare opportunity.

Ice Chewing Records 316

— Bing

In today's society, only a certain kind of people can distinguish class consciousness most clearly, that is, the tea room colleagues in hotels, bathhouses, companies, and institutions. If you ask them about the people who pass before their eyes every day, who is three points higher and nine percent lower than whom in terms of status and wealth, I guarantee that they will answer very accurately.

One day, a large crab and a small crab were arguing. It was because the large crab was teaching the small crab, who refused to obey. The large crab said, "Son, why do you always walk sideways? Why don't you be more disciplined and walk straight forward?" The small crab replied with disdain, "I'll ask my father!" The large crab raised its toes, but limped and dared not move. It turned out that it had always only

Page 22

knew how to walk sideways. There are many fathers in the world who walk sideways without restraint, wanting people, celebrities, but they always teach their children and descendants to walk straight, which is as comical as the large crab.

Recently, I moved to Baoshan Road, the frontline of the Shanghai war. I run around every day among the broken walls and rubble, and found a place where I really need to thank the Japanese. The original towering buildings have now become shelters for the poor. Whenever a storm comes, the poor don't have to worry about not having a place to hide. Especially in the evening, you can only see the dark groups of beggars, small people following adults, hunchbacks and pale faces, surging in and out of those broken eaves like tides. If this were before the "January 28th" incident, the poor would not have had such an active and free opportunity? Isn't this the grace of the Japanese? I should express my gratitude here on their behalf! Alas, eaters!

I seem to have heard many adults and gentlemen say that the Chinese nation has laid a solid foundation that is unyielding. Although it has been conquered by foreign races many times in history, the result has always been that the foreign races were assimilated. Now things are a bit different, or the foundation has changed direction. Let me use a small thing to speak. Our modern clothing, since the Western style came, needless to say, new-style figures all regard wearing Western clothes as etiquette, and even old-fashioned people are also trying it out like monkeys wearing colored jackets. Such Westernization is ironclad proof that they have been assimilated by foreign races. Only the Japanese and Indians can still maintain their inherent national spirit. Look at the ordinary Japanese who always wear kimonos, and the Indians who always can't bear to part with their national cloaks, even though they are already slaves of a fallen country. This is indeed a small thing, and the people of the country should also know to be vigilant.

Farewell, Nanjing

Farewell, Nanjing, full of melancholy, looking back with extra affection, pitiable is the color of the stars and moon, long shining on the sounds of pipes and strings, happy land without soldiers, official field with war, Rehe frequently reports emergency, how to comfort the peace,

Last night I had a dream: a group of people surrounded a young man who had attempted suicide, and one of them was reprimanding the young man: "Now is the time when the nation and the country are in trouble, how can you play this kind of useless trick! "Sketches in the Classroom" 318

— Chen Diqing

Ding! Ding! Ding! This is -- the academy's afternoon one o'clock class bell, it has already rung. One by one the students walked into the classroom, still holding a Western-style book in their hands, so we know this is an English class.

More and more students, in the whole classroom, a kind of noisy, lively, chaotic, crazy laughter, clucking, ... sound comes out, the procedure is very chaotic.

English professor Mr. Wu came, wearing a black-grey long robe, with tortoiseshell glasses on, not very tall, or even a little shorter than ordinary people, looking like a young man in his twenties. When he saw the classroom door, to be honest, he seemed a little scared, and his two eyes, covered by tortoiseshell glasses, were always rolling left and right. However, when he stepped onto the platform, he smiled again, this smile seemed like a lovely expression to the students in the hall.

"Dear students, please be quiet, don't talk," Mr. Wu said in a very weak voice and very gently after he got on the platform:

The air in the classroom told us that today's class was indeed different from the usual class. Every student's mind was looking forward to, expecting, a kind of major problem that they wanted to say but dared not say. The words of the teacher, which were ineffective in ordinary times, were particularly effective today. Although the voice was so weak, it immediately calmed the noisy, chaotic classroom. Every student stared blankly, hoping to solve this major problem.

"Ha! Ha! Why are you all here so early today?" Mr. Wu seemed very happy and said this again, making all the students in the hall laugh.

Water Cutoff by the Private Water Company 319

"Mr. Wu! Don't you know? The school is holding monthly exams next week. Everyone is here today hoping you can give us a topic." A student seemed to be answering, and everyone applauded.

"Oh! So that's how it is! Ha! Ha!..." Mr. Wu laughed, and the whole hall burst into wild laughter and applause.

"Mr. Wu! What will the exam be like this time! Let's do it the same way as before! Please give us a topic quickly, so we can prepare, prepare,..." Another student stood up and said, followed by another round of applause.

"Of course, the same way as before."

"Hurry! Hurry, give us the topic!"

"Okay! Okay! Everyone, don't make noise, I still have something to say to you! Regarding this exam, you should understand my difficulties. When doing anything, you should consider both sides, so that both sides can benefit. For example, in the previous few exams, I gave you the topics one or two weeks in advance. Although it was beneficial to you, it was not good for me as a teacher. It would either be said that I was too careless, or that I was too sloppy. Isn't that just considering your side! So, no matter what, I can't give you the topic this time, so I can consider..."

"No! No!" Mr. Wu hadn't finished speaking, and there were many voices of opposition saying:

"Opposition! Opposition!"

"Absolutely not! Absolutely not!"

"Absolutely against! Absolutely against!" In this mixed opposition, there were also clucking, banging... floor noises, table noises, whistle noises...

"Everyone, don't make noise, don't quarrel, I haven't finished speaking yet!... A student listened and suddenly became a little quieter again. Mr. Wu continued, "There is one more thing, didn't the Ministry of Education send someone to investigate last year? At the same time, there was a kind of bad criticism, saying that the grades of our school's students are too bad, too careless. This kind of criticism not only hinders the school's reputation, but also greatly affects your future. Therefore, no matter what, you have to bite the bullet and ask for some knowledge, which will be a tool for you to do things in the future. So, from now on, don't be too careless about the exams. No matter what, I can't give you the topic this time; however, regarding the scores, I can be a little more lenient when I grade the papers, and just make sure you pass..."

"Okay! Since Mr. Wu won't give us the topic, then please draw a scope for us." A student was moved by the teacher's words and made a request.

Mr. Wu had no choice but to agree to the student's second request. However, Mr. Wu declared again that you must keep it a secret, so that you won't tell the other students, teachers, or people outside.

Shop Assistant Communication

Articles and Submissions 321

Editor: Laborers, shop assistants, and apprentices under the iron heel of capitalism have always had to silently endure everything from their employers, with little opportunity to participate in opinions. Therefore, the labor-capital divide is very distinct, and all the doubts and hidden pains of shop assistants have no way to be resolved or vented. Since your esteemed publication opened the shop assistant communication column, you have painstakingly and meticulously answered the questions and difficulties of shop assistants; this spirit of serving society and benefiting the masses is truly worthy of our praise and gratitude. Now I have a question, please grant me an answer:

I am an apprentice at ×× Industrial Company in this city. When I left school and entered this company, many classmates congratulated me in unison, and even the teacher who introduced me said, "This company's management is so good, its methods are so good, its business is so prosperous, and its treatment is so generous. You have a future full of hope in this company!" Who knew that the reality was far from it, this company is just living up to its reputation in vain:

Time has passed like a monotonous three years, and I, who was full of hope, have become a disappointed youth. Although my age is constantly increasing, I am still engaged in a delivery career (my position is delivering packages, so I am also known as the package delivery apprentice). In these three years, apart from receiving a bonus of six dollars, the remaining few dollars of monthly salary are sometimes deducted due to leave taken for weddings, funerals, or illnesses. Now I am already twenty-one years old, sir, how can I face my parents, how can I face myself!

Now, for the sake of the company's bright future and driven by my own ambition, I would like to make the following contributions to the new manager; our youth leave their parents and hometowns to study commerce far away. The reason is to learn a skill to earn a living, to serve society, and to support our families. Therefore, the manager is like a second parent to the apprentices; the master instructors have the responsibility of teaching the apprentices. Now, we dozens of apprentices, in addition to completing twelve hours of delivery work, have no other training or teaching. Therefore, after three years, we are still the same as before, and we still do not understand business conditions or experience. This is detrimental to both the future of the apprentices and the company itself. I would like to ask the new manager to pay attention to this point.

The company's business has always been managed by the manager alone, and the heads of each department are just the manager's eyes and ears. Although there have been several reorganizations, it is always the same old soup.

Page 23

Therefore, our promotion depends entirely on the director's joy or anger. Nowadays, "flattery," which is recognized as one of the arts of dealing with people in the 20th century, is indeed an excellent shortcut to seek promotion, but how many of us apprentices who have not been in the world for long understand it? Moreover, "those with ambition are ashamed to flatter," right? Therefore, there are many people who remain apprentices even after studying for three or four years (I am one of them). As for the director, because they mostly came from "flattery," they only seek to increase their own salary and stabilize their position, and they do not hesitate to be accomplices, treating lower-level colleagues harshly. For example, holding salespeople responsible for out-of-stock items is one of their clever tricks to curry favor. The manager listens to the director without question. After the January 28th Incident, they did not hesitate to reduce the salaries of the younger employees by ten or twenty dollars in the name of austerity to increase the salary of the director who earns nearly one hundred dollars a month, causing widespread resentment and people harboring the intention to leave. However, the manager insisted on courteous reception and clear inventory. I would like to ask the new manager to correct this kind of superficial treatment that does not address the root cause and forces people to do the impossible.

It is said that the interior is going to be expanded, according to news from senior staff, new employees will be recruited, but the apprentices will remain unchanged. Sir, this is so bitter for us apprentices, are we supposed to be apprentices until we die? Regarding the duties of a salesperson, apprentices can handle about half of them. If we are given a ten-dollar salary to do a job that is worth more than ten dollars, we would be truly grateful. What could be better? Moreover, people from outside the company may not be able to handle the duties in our company because they have to manage inventory, keep accounts, and other extra work. Now, instead of using the people we have, we are seeking help from outside. I really don't want this policy of abandoning the fundamental and pursuing the superficial to be realized. For the sake of the future of many comrades, I would like to ask the new manager to adopt my humble opinion:

I originally wanted to write the above opinions directly to the manager, but after thinking carefully, if my enthusiasm is appreciated, that would be fine, but if I accidentally offend his dignity, then being fired is a small matter, and I would also be labeled as a reactionary, which I dare not accept! Finally, I want to state to you, sir, that I am not fabricating facts or attacking others, but I am relying entirely on the dictates of my conscience to urge the manager to awaken and to make a cry for our comrades who are experiencing the same situation. Sir, I think you will certainly not reject me because of the imperfection of my writing, right?

I wish you well.

Sincerely,

Lu Yiping, an apprentice

Editor's note: Mr. Lu is an employee of the well-known × National Products Company in this city. Recently, we have received letters from employees of this company several times, all unanimously complaining. This proves that Mr. Lu's statement of "widespread resentment, and people harboring the intention to leave" is indeed not fabricated. In order to hope that this relatively well-established national products company will flourish, we also take advantage of the opportunity of the new manager's arrival to introduce Mr. Lu's submission to him.

Mr. Lu's first suggestion is to give apprentices a real opportunity to practice. On this point, we can look at the post office, which is still under foreign management in fact. They rotate every newly arrived low-level employee to practice in various departments; therefore, after a year, they can roughly know the overall situation.

His second suggestion is that the manager should have a more accurate observation of the assessment of lower-level employees. This seems difficult to do; because the manager has to manage all the affairs of the store, he naturally has to rely on middle-level employees as his eyes and ears for the assessment of lower-level employees. But now that it has come to "widespread resentment, and people harboring the intention to leave," it is obvious that the work of middle-level employees has its own unfairness. In order to stabilize the overall situation of the store, it is necessary to steal some time from the busy schedule and investigate it yourself. On the one hand, you can promote some talented people, and on the other hand, you can find out and punish some unfair middle-level employees.

His third suggestion is that when the company expands, if it needs employees, it should promote as many apprentices as possible. This is really right. We hope that the new manager originally intended to do so, but due to the miscommunication of senior staff, it caused Mr. Lu's anxiety. If the communication is not mistaken, then it is really necessary to cancel the original plan and adopt Mr. Lu's suggestion.

Novel

Fleeting Time in a Dream (Sixteenth Installment) 322

— Qin Shouou

(9) Marriage and Principles

The climate of the western United States is indeed drier and clearer than other places in the temperate zone. After muddling through three years at the University of California, Wu Yi really didn't want to return to Shanghai, surrounded by a damp air. However, a voluminous doctoral dissertation had been created with painstaking effort, and a diploma worth dozens of times more than gold had also been received as scheduled. The purpose of gilding was achieved, so what was the point of lingering in the United States? Wu Yi wasn't a fool!

When Wu Yi set off from Seattle to return to China, he first called Wang Yulin to report his itinerary; he hoped that as soon as the ship arrived in Shanghai, he could meet his three old friends whom he had been separated from for a long time at the pier. However, the result was very embarrassing for him. Only a group of dockworkers he didn't know came to the pier to welcome him that day. The three old friends were nowhere to be seen.

"Wang Mansion? Please let Lawyer Wang speak!" In a mood of extreme anger, Wu Yi suppressed his anger and went straight to × Hotel. After checking into a room, he was busy calling Wang Yulin's office. The reply was "Lawyer Wang is at home," so Wu Yi immediately inquired at Wang Mansion again.

"Ah! Dr. Wu? It's unfortunate today, my wife just gave birth at home, and I couldn't come to the pier to pick you up! Please forgive me! Are you angry?" Wang Yulin appeared on the phone, speaking extremely hastily. "At this moment, the child has not yet landed. Are you in room 305 of × Hotel? I will definitely come! Please forgive me! Please forgive me!"

Only then did Wu Yi relieve half of his anger, and happily put down the phone. At the same time, he recalled the wedding photo that Yulin had sent him last spring. He hurriedly opened his suitcase and rummaged through it, and finally found it.

"Ah! What a beautiful wife!" A petite, graceful, and generous bride appeared in the photo, causing Wu Yi to praise involuntarily. Although he had seen it once, he only noticed Wang Yulin's good fortune when he looked at it again now. He held this eight-inch photo and sat quietly in a daze, as calm as someone who had lived in Shanghai for a long time.

More than an hour later, Wang Yulin indeed rushed over in disheveled clothes, his demeanor as excited as if he had drunk alcohol.

"Hello! Old Wu! I am extremely happy today!" He sat down on the table, his face full of smiles. "You have come, and I have also given birth to a son, isn't this double the happiness!"

"Congratulations! Congratulations! I simply rushed back specifically to congratulate you!" Wu Yi also smiled. "But Zhao Qianli, has he sent me letters recently, where is he at the moment? After the Da Wang Company closed down, where did our Lin Daping go?"

When Lin Daping was mentioned, Yulin seemed very unhappy and immediately stopped smiling. However, he did not disappoint Wu Yi and still faithfully told him about the recent situation of Lin Daping and Zhao Qianli. Only then did Wu Yi know that Zhao Qianli had received extremely satisfactory results from the lengthy discussions he had published in the newspaper on weekdays ten days ago, and had gone to Hankou as the director of the Public Works Bureau. For some reason, Lin Daping had also become a famous lawyer at sea. Although Mai'e had died, he had married another opera singer and was living a very comfortable life, and also had a car with a number of four "fives." Unfortunately, according to Yulin, he also had some of the arrogance of a petty man who had achieved success, as arrogant as if he thought the world was his alone. No wonder Yulin had notified him of Wu Yi's arrival, but he turned a deaf ear.
